À ǹsiı̄ nsāŋ kòp mbɔ̂m.
À ǹsinda mɛ lı̀ɓay.
À ǹsiŋha mɛ ŋgàndàk hı̀ɔ̀mi; dı̀ ǹsiŋha diɔ̀mi.
À ǹsiŋhaha nyuu; ɓòdàa ɓa nsı̄ŋhaha mɓòŋ.
À ǹsit mbambà nɛ̀y.
À ǹsiyha mɛ ŋgı̀m sɛ̀l mbɔt; dı̀ ǹsiyha mbɔt yes.
À ǹsı̂gha mɛ̀ njɛ̀l yaŋgà.
À nsı̀nda koo wee isı̄ lɛ ndı̀ŋ.
À nsı̀nda makòo sı̄ lɛ ndı̀ŋ ndı̀ŋ!
À nsı̄ndil kòò u walōm.
À nsı̄ŋhana nyuu nı̀ kusa; ɓa nsı̄ŋhana mambus.
À nsı̄t ɓôt mbòŋ.
À nsı̄t mɛ mbɔ̀m; à nsı̄t mɛ mbòŋ.
À ǹsôblɛ nyɛ bı̀kwèè, màkɔ̀ŋ, màlep.
À ǹsoghà.
À ǹsoghak nyɛ nı̀ hɔp.
À nsōgol mis.
À ǹsok sǔglù inyùu ndı̀ŋhà yèe.
À ǹsôlha mɛ màlêt yàŋgà; dı̀ ǹsôlha nyɛ.
À nsòmbol ɓebha ɓes wɛ̀.
À nsòmbol libla ŋgwee.
À ǹsômha mɛ kòò i ɓɛ̄ɛ; dı̀ ǹsômha dikòò ces i ndɔ̀ndɔ̀k.
À nsòmol ɓoŋgō i lı̀pɔ̀ndɔ.
À ǹsonōl nyɛ ikède ndāp.
À ǹsoŋglaha mɛ kààt; dı̀ nsōŋglaha kaàt.
À nsòò liɛk li ye nyɛ i nyɔ̀.
À ǹsoō mɔnı̄; ɓa nsòo màm ɓa mɓɔ̂ŋ.
À nsòògɛnɛ laŋ i mbàmbà.
À nsōohana man i mbēdge.
À nsòoo nsugi.
À ǹsoōs ɓâs i sûp.
À ǹsos mût mɔ̀k.
À ǹsɔ mān lı̀wàghà.
À ǹsɔ mān lı̀wàhgà.
À nsɔ̄dlɛ njɛɛ ŋgāa?
À ǹsɔ̂hbɛnɛ mɛ̂.
À nsɔ̀k mɛ hı̄ı̄ hɔ̀ma.
À ǹsɔlɔ̀p.
À ǹsɔ̂m lilàŋ i kɔ̄lâ.
À ǹsɔ̂m wɔɔ i ŋwı̀ı̀.
À ǹsɔmb hivɛ̀ɛ̀vɛɛ liɓàdò.
À ǹsɔmb nugā i gweē ǹsòn nı̀ ǹsòn.
À ǹsɔ̂mda nyɛ i mɔ̀ɔ.
À ǹsɔmōl tɛl yee.
À nsɔ̄ngɔl bikààt.
À ǹsɔŋ yaga nyɔɔ̄ likɔ̀mb li nyòl.
À ǹsɔ̂p malep ù ǹti nyɛ.
À nsɔ̄s nugā.
À nsūdɛ ɓe u.
À ǹsudɛ wɔɔ.
À ǹsuɛ̄nɛ mɛ màlêt.
À ǹsuɛ̄nɛ nyuu yeē.
À ǹsûgɓaha mɛ màsɔ̀ŋ, dı̀ ǹsûgɓaha masɔ̀ŋ.
À nsùgdɛ mâm ma kwâŋ.
À ǹsûgdɛ nyɛ.
À nsugi, ɓàhlɛ mɛ̀ nyɛ!
À nsùgul bijɛk.
À nsùgul moo i nhɔ̀n.
À ǹsugus dilɔ cee hana isı̄.
À ǹsûhha mɛ hı̀kòa ŋgwee, dı̀ ǹsûhha hikòa.
À nsùhul nyuu.
À ǹsul mɛ ŋgɔ̀nd.
À ǹsulha mɛ mǎŋkeē ŋgı̀m ǹtomba, dı̀ bisūlha nyɛ mı̀ntomba.
À ǹsulul ŋwaa njàŋgi.
À ǹsûm ŋkòò i jɔ̀ɔ.
À ǹsûmblɛ kondòm.
À ǹsûmha mɛ tèk mɛ̀tama, tɛhɛ kı̀i ɓa nsùmha hisi.
À ǹsûmha nyɛ ŋ̀kòò i jɔ̀ɔ, dı̀ ǹsûmha miŋkòò i ɓòɓôk.
À ǹsûndlaha mɛ̂ ŋ̀kòò, dı̀ ǹsûndlaha ŋgolı̂.
À ǹsundūl mɛ mı̀nsı̀ŋgà mi bitamb.
À ǹsunhɛnɛ ŋ̀ɛm nı̀ màlep.
À nsùŋul ŋwaa inyùulɛ̄ à ǹloōha nlam.
À ǹsuū sâŋ.
À ǹsuūlaha mɛ nyǒy, nyǒy iɓâ i nsuūlaha mɛ̂.
À ǹta mɛ jàm.
À ntààyɛ kı̀i kɔ̄ɔ.
À ǹtablaha mɛ pɔɔ, dı̀ ǹtablaha mapɔɔ mes.
À ǹtagɓɛ wɛ̂swɛ̀s!
À ntāhɓɛnɛ mɛ̂.
À ǹtamba bijɛk, bı̀jɛk bi ntambâ.
À ǹtaŋ lɛ nyɛ ɓe nyɛn à biɓāda mɔnı̄.
À ǹteblaha nyɛ ŋgı̀m kı̂sı̀n, dı̀ ǹteblaha mandap mes.
À ǹtêdɓa i ŋgɔ̀k.
À ǹtedha mɛ mı̀ntomba, dı̀ ǹtedha mintomba.
À ǹtee miŋkɔ̀ŋgɔ̀ mû mbɔt yee yɔsɔ̂ à ǹsiyâ.
À ǹteēaha mɛ pebee, dı̀ ǹteēaha pebee.
À ǹteēɓaha mɛ ɓɔ̀blà.
À ǹteeda ŋgweya u nyik.
À ǹteeha mɛ bı̀lı̀m, dı̀ ǹteeha bilı̀m.
À ǹteeha mɛ ŋgàndàk bı̀jɛk, dı̀ ǹteeha kilɔ̂k yes lɛ̀n.
À ǹtees mɛ kùù.
À ǹtegēl mɛ̂ inyùu hı̀hòhà hyee.
À ǹtegel sɛ̂l yee i ndɔ̀bɔ̀.
À ǹtegha mɛ têblè i ndɔ̀bɔ̀, dı̀ ǹtegha bitêblè.
A ǹtegi diɓɛ̀ɛ cagācàgà.
À ǹteglaha mɛ hı̀ɓɛ̀ɛ ŋgı̀ ɓɛl, dı̀ ǹteglaha diɓɛ̀ɛ.
À ǹtêndha mɛ̂ ǹlòŋ ŋ̀kɔda, dı̀ ǹtêndha minlòŋ ŋwes.
À ǹtêŋɓaha lilàŋ, ɓa ntêŋɓaha malàŋ.
À ǹteŋēp ni ɓòlo.
À ǹtɛhɛ biyı̌ndà.
À ǹtɛhɛ mɛ̂ à tagɓɛ mɓàyoŋgo.
À ntɛ̄hnà ɓe, à yè mùt ndim, nùt mùt à ntɛ̄hna lɛ!
À ǹtɛlɓɛnɛ i ŋgı̀i nàŋ.
À ǹtɛlɛp bikēehɛnɛ.
À ǹtɛlɛ̂p ndigi wɛ̀ɛ̀ sisiŋ.
À ǹti mɛ bı̀tamb gwee à têmb à tɔɔ̄.
À ǹti mɛ gwàt bi maɔ̀k.
À ǹti mɛ kɔ̄p malep ma mbondō.
À ǹti mɛ làgà i dikoo ditân.
À ǹti mɛ ŋgumà kɛl.
À ǹti wɛ dı̀sɔɔ caŋɛn?
À ǹtiblɛ nyɛ màɓuy.
À ǹtihil mɛ i ŋɔ.
À ntı̄bil ɓôt nı̀ hyaŋhanjèk.
À ntı̄blana koyōp licɛ̀ɛ.
À ǹtı̂dha mɛ ǹtùbà ŋgı̀ mı̀nsòa, dı̀ ǹtı̂dha makɔ̀ndɔ̀ mes.
À ǹtı̂glaha mɛ̂ ǹsugi.
À ntı̀ı̀ ntı̀ı̂k.
À ǹtı̂lɓaha mɛ ı̄ ntōŋ Presbı̀teriɛ̀n; dı̀ bitı̀lɓaha i ntōŋ.
À ǹtı̂lha mɛ kààt yàŋgà; dı̀ ǹtı̂lha bikààt.
À ntı̄ndɓà wɛ̀ɛ kidı̂k i ŋkɔ̀k lɛ i mɓı̄iŋgɛ̀.
À ǹtı̂ŋhaha mɛ lı̀kè.
À ǹtı̂ŋlaha mɛ ɓòò nyɔɔ i sūdɓeŋ; dı̀ ǹtı̂ŋlaha bilem gwes.
À ǹtı̂p lɔ̂.
À ǹtobha mɛ jàm mɛ̀ ŋ̀koōbà ɓe; dı̀ ǹtobha maŋwı̀n.
À ǹtôdha mɛ ŋgèdà ŋgı̀ kɔ̀là; dı̀ ǹtôdha i ǹlèlèm ŋgɛŋ.
À ntòhol tibı̄ biwàdà.
À ǹtolɓa ɓeba mbɛgɛ̀ɛ̀.
À ǹtolha komōl bisɛ̀l bi ɓɔŋgɛ.
À ǹtolha mɛ̂ bı̀ɓòò bi bikı̀dà; dı̀ ǹtolha bijɛk gwes.
À ǹtolos bisiŋli gwee.
À ntòmdɛnɛ i tı̀sɔ̀n lı̀hala.
À ǹtômlaha mɛ̂ ŋ̀ɔ matɛ̄bɛ̂l; dı̀ ntòmlaha ɓatɔ̀nɛ̀.
À ǹtôndlaha mɛ nyùu; ɓòdàa ɓa ntôndlaha manyùu.
À ǹtonha mɛ pên i mbōt.
À ǹtonol nyɛ tèk i màmaŋ inyùulɛ̄ à ŋkɔ̀n dikɔlâ.
À ntòŋgol ɓɔn ɓee lɔ̄ŋgɛ̂.
À ǹtooha mɛ kɔ̀ɔ̀ ǹtomba; dı̀ ǹtooha mintomba ŋwes.
À ǹtoōha mɛ mbòŋ ɓàtòlò nı̀ mɔ̀ɔ.
À ǹtop hyembi; mɛ̀ ǹtop nyɛ jǒl.
À ntɔ̀ ntɔ̀ɔ̂k.
À ntɔ̀hɓa nı̀ tawèdè.
À ǹtɔhla i ŋgı̀i jǎŋgòlò à kwɔ̂.
À ǹtɔhɔl mɛ ı̄ mɔ̀ɔ̀ ma ɓàɓɔ̀ŋ ɓeba.
À ntɔ̀n mbɔt ɓa njoà.
À ǹtɔn mɛ mbɔ̄t ni pên.
À ǹtɔ̂ndlɛ mɛ jı̌s.
À ntɔ̀ŋ hɔsı̀ yee.
À ntɔ̄ŋ mɛ jùu ni ŋwày.
À ǹtɔ̂ŋ wɛ bı̀jɛk.
À ǹtɔɔ mɛ̂ ı̀ kɛ̀ pam i wɔ̌m.
À ntɔ̄p ɓe kɔhɔl hiyèyeē hyee.
À ntɔ̄p ɓe ŋwı̀n û ; yàk wɛ̀ tɔp lɛ ndèk !
À ǹtulha mɛ bı̀ɓòò bi mibâ; dı̀ ǹtulha mibâ.
À ǹtulul mɛ sɛ̀l i mâŋ.
À ǹtumbā mbɛ̂k; ŋgǎn nyɛ̀mb ı̀ ǹtumbà.
À ntùmbha mɛ màkòò isı̄; ɓa ntùmbha makòò.
À ǹtûmbna hɛɛ?
À ǹtuŋha i pɔɔ.
À ntūs hida hı̄ lisàaga.
À ǹtus mɛ tàmba i mɔ̀ɔ.
À ǹwaŋ moo lât.
À ǹyaba i wı̌p, ɓa ɛp nyɛ̄ nsɛ̀m!
À ńyābdana ması̂ŋ.
À ńyādap.
À ńyādap ǹten liyadɓàk.
À ńyādɓɛnɛ jol li Yesù.
À nyaŋglak ndigi bı̄ bı̀jɛk, à ǹjɛ ɓe gwɔ.
À ńyèèmbaha biɓòlo gwee; à ńyèèmbaha mɔɔ mee.
À ńyèènɛ i jı̀ibɛ̀.
À ǹyeēnɛ malep; ù ńyèènɛ hɛɛ?
À ǹyegla mɛ mɔ̀ni.
À ńyègle ni ŋ̀kɔ̀ŋ.
À nyehi kı̀i ǹsùhlàgà.
À ǹyek yaga ɓahɔ̀ma ɓa ntòl, à ǹnyɔdɓɛnɛ mɛ hāna i mbɔ̀m.
À ńyèmb nyɔ̂.
À ńyèmbi nyɔ̂.
À ǹyên à nnigı̂p.
À ǹyên lɛ hı̀s!
À ǹyenēs ɓɔŋgɛ inyùu ŋgı̀ mànoglà wǎp.
À ǹyêŋha mɛ ŋ̀ɔ, ɓa ńyêŋha miŋɔ.
À ǹyeŋı̄ ŋɔ.
À ǹyɛ̂gɓɛnɛ i tūŋ ndāp.
À ńyɛ̀na mâm; à ǹyɛ nyɛ̄ màm.
À ǹyidɛ̄ manyâŋ gwàlâk.
À ǹyidɛ̄ mbambà ı̀ m̂pàn nı̀ nɛ̀y.
À ǹyiga cɔɔ̀gɛ̀ lı̀sɛ̀ɛ, à tagɓɛ̀.
À ǹyigha mɛ tàmba; dı̀ ǹyigha biɓɔ̀t.
À ǹyilā ɓeba mût.
À ǹyilı̄s nyuu yeē tɔ̀ jàm.
À nyimbil moo.
À ńyı̄ biɓòlo.
À ńyı̄ ɓihı̄l mâm.
À ńyı̄ cɔ màɓam.
À ńyı̄ lep pesɛ.
À ńyı̄ mahɔp mmaà.
À ńyı̄ minsɔn.
À ńyı̄ nyɔgı̄.
À ńyı̄ ŋgwɛɛ̀gɛ̀.
À ńyı̄ŋha mɛ bı̀kààt à bitēedà; dı̀ ǹyiŋha wɛ ɓès ɓɔɓasô.
À ǹyı̂s man i têblè.
À ǹyodɛ̄ man hana isı̄.
À ǹyôglaha mɛ yāŋan kɔgā, dı̀ ǹyôglaha maɓɛ̀l ma liɓɛ̀m.
À ǹyonos biaâ.
À ńyōnos ɓe masàŋ me.
À ǹyoŋōl sagi liɓɔ̄ŋ.
À ǹyɔbna i òt mı̀nsɔ̀ŋgi.
À ǹyɔbɔ̄l ndêk.
À ńyɔ̄dɓɛnɛ mɛ̂.
À ǹyɔgɔ̄l mɛ lı̀ɓɔŋ.
À ǹyɔ̂ŋ nyɛ bı̀hiŋ.
À ǹyɔŋā maŋgɛ mudàa.
À ńyɔ̀ɔ̀mbana mɛ̂.
À ǹyubdaha mɛ̀ mı̀nsɔ̀ŋgi.
À ǹyubɛ̄ likɔ̀ndɔ̀ i mòo.
À ǹyûbha mɛ màkòò malēp màsuni.
À ǹyugūl nsòn nugā.
À ńyùmbɛ ɓep nyɔ̂.
À ǹyûmbnɛ mɛ mbɔ̄t i ŋgı̀ı̀.
À ńyūyi kı̀i mǎn nyùu.
À ŋ̀ablɛ pee nı̀ ǹtàndàà kek.
À ŋāŋ kaàt màua.
À ŋ̀ebna mɛ kààt i tùŋ yeē.
À ŋ̀ebna mɛ kààt inyùu wɔ̀ŋi.
À ŋēdɛ mɛ wı̌p.
À ŋ̀êdha nyɛ màɓàdò ma ŋwɛmɛl.
À ŋ̀edlaha mɛ kɔ̄ɔ̄ i ɛ̄.
À ŋ̀êgɓaha nyɛ liɓāy.
À ŋègel mɛ inyùu bı̀jɛk.
À ŋ̀embes miŋkùmɛ̀ ɓòo.
À ŋgeŋgi nı̀ mbɔt.
À ŋgɛ̄ŋɛl i ɓòlo ini.
À ŋ̀gɔŋ mangɛ.
À ŋ̀gwandɛ mɛ hāna liɓōk lini!
À ŋ̀gwelel i njɛ̌l dɔ̂ktà.
À ŋ̀gweŋgɛ dikàhà mu njɛ̀l!
À ŋgwēs à nnùnɓa i lèman.
À ŋgwēs à ntɛ̀ɛ̀hɛ pebee.
À ŋgwēs minsɔ̀gâ.
À ŋgwēs nyɛ ı̀ lɔ̀ɔ̀ ɓěs.
À ŋgwēs ŋgɔgɔ̀l.
À ŋ̀gwɛ̂l mût wı̌p lɛ ɓàndàmm.
À ŋ̀gwı̂nɓɛnɛ nyɛ nlōm njɛ̌l.
À ŋgwò lând.
À ŋ̀hangap i pōla yâp i sèk jɔ̀mɔ̂l.
À ŋkà bisɛ̀l.
À ŋ̀kaa jɛ̄.
À ŋ̀kabdɛ ki ı̀ gwaŋan gwɔm.
À ŋ̀kadā muy i ndāp.
À ŋ̀kagâl maŋ mût.
À ŋ̀kagap ni i kàgà ye.
À ŋ̀kahal kàgda ni ǹsɔn.
À ŋ̀kahal kòhlɛ gwɔm gwee.
À ŋ̀kahal ni hyɛ̀lɛ̀l.
À ŋ̀kâk lɛ à nlɔ̀ kı̀.
À ŋ̀kak moo.
À ŋ̀kâl wɛ m̂paha.
À ŋ̀kan mbɔt wap.
À ŋkàŋ ɓaɓɔ̀blà nı̀ njùu.
À ŋkàp ŋgandàk.
À ŋ̀kât mût njèk.
À ŋ̀kât ŋkɔ̀ŋ.
À ŋkègsɛ maŋgɛ sǔglù.
À ŋ̀kêmhɛ̄ i jàm mɛ̀ m̂pɔt.
À ŋ̀kenɛ̄ ni ŋgên!
À ŋ̀keŋēl mɛ jɔ̀mb li bisiŋgli.
À ŋ̀key liɓàdò mbɔ̄ŋgɔ.
À ŋ̀keyɛ mɛ ŋgwɔ̄ kı̀i mɛ̀ m̂pam i nyɛ̄nı̄.
À ŋkɛ̀.
À ŋkɛ̀ à ncēbdà.
À ŋkɛ̀ à nhı̀ga higā hı̀gà.
À ŋkɛ̀ à nhùdà.
À ŋkɛ̀ à ŋkwāŋ mu ı̄ mbedge? mbegde?
À ŋkɛ̀ bisày; à ŋkɛ̀ i lāp bisày.
À ŋkɛ̀ ɓonaɓona.
À ŋkɛ̀ hɛɛ? ù nlòl hɛɛ?
À ŋkɛ̀ hiahı̀à wɛ̀ɛ ŋwàa ǹyèe.
À ŋkɛ̀ hyɛbɛdhyɛ̀bɛ̀t.
À ŋkɛ̀ hyɛbhyɛ̀p.
À ŋkɛ̀ hyɛ̂bhyɛ̀p.
À ŋkɛ̀ i kı̀nda.
À ŋ̀kɛ i mbòo mɔ̀ni.
À ŋ̀kɛ̂ i yūugà ɓàkɔ̀kɔ̂n.
À ŋ̀kɛ ı̄ kwàk makɔ̀ndɔ̀.
À ŋkɛ̀ jebjep ?
À ŋkɛ̀ jwɛɛ̀.
À ŋ̀kɛ māɓɛda.
À ŋkɛ̀ ŋgaŋgàà wɛ̀ɛ kàgàà.
À ŋ̀kɛ̂ sǔglù i mbɛ̀ŋgɛ̀ ɓàkana.
À ŋkɛ̀ wɛ̌ŋgɔ̀ŋlɛ yòŋgoo.
À ŋkɛ̀ɛ à mɓàghɛ munu i njɛ̌l.
À ŋ̀kɛnɛ̀k, à ɓuŋgûl, nyɛ kı̀ nunu.
À ŋ̀kɛt hiyɛŋ.
À ŋkɛ̄y malep.
À ŋ̀kit ɓɛs.

Ɓànigı̂l mbàŋgo ɓa ŋkòŋoo ni ndɔ̀ndɔ̀k.
Ɓanjı̄ɓɔ à nlɛ̀t.
Ɓànyàndom ɓa nsɔ̀là.
Ɓànyàŋ ɓa makàbò ɓa negâ.
Ɓànyàŋ ɓa ncı̂lha ɓɔn ɓap meè.
Ɓànyɔ màɔ̀k ɓa mɓūgla mbondō màɔ̀k.
Ɓànyɔ màɔ̀k ɓa ŋàgna ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓàŋ mbɔk..
Ɓaŋâl mı̌s.
Ɓàŋga ɓaŋgā.
Ɓàŋga ini i ńyàŋ mɛ ŋɛ̄m.
Ɓàŋga lègel lɛ m̂ɓɔ̀ɔ̀ lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Ɓàŋga mǎn ɓàsàa ı̀ni.
Ɓàŋga mùdàa ı̀ nlama ɓe ɓɛp yên.
Ɓàŋga mùt ı̀ ŋàgɓà ɓee.
Ɓàŋga yɔŋ i ye ɓɛ̄.
Ɓaŋgâl lı̀ɓàdò, ɓaŋgâl mbɔt.
Ɓàŋwɛ̀kŋwɛ̀k ɓa ntòl i ŋgèdà mbèŋ.
Ɓàɔŋ tɔ̄ŋ ɓa nhèmblaha mamaŋ; à ǹhêmblaha mɛ gwāŋan bitamb.
Ɓap cǎy di makɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Ɓap mùt ɓɛ̀l.
Ɓàpàgi ɓa mâl mɛ màkɔ̀ndɔ̀ lɛ ɓàm.
Ɓàpodôl ɓa ɓe tɛhɛ̂ nı̀ pɔt bı̀nděē.
Ɓàpòma ɓa nnum ɓe ŋgandàk i ŋwı̀i unu.
Ɓàpùma mɛ̀ ǹjɛ ɓa nnyı̀s mɛ ŋgàndàk.
Ɓas hı̀kèŋ.
Ɓas i hyɔbı̄ i ŋadap nyɛ ha i kòo.
Ɓàs i mɓômb lɛ̂n i ɓòm.
Ɓàs i nnyɔŋyɛnɛ inyùu ɓēba yee nlamb.
Ɓàs i nsɔɔ̀.

Ɓas lı̀kɔa.

Ɓàsàa ɓa binɔ̄lna ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓàsàa ɓa mɓèna kâl lɛ ndàlàl ı̀ yè kɔ̀n u mahindi.
Ɓàsàa ɓa mpɔ̄t lɛ ɓàɛ̀mb nı̀ mı̀ŋkugı̀ bi ntɛ̄hnana mu ɓāŋgɛ̀gɛà.
Ɓàsàa ɓa njɛ̄ ɓe hitatmbāy.
Ɓàsàa ɓa njòna lɔŋgɛ̂.
Ɓàsàa ɓa ńyànna ŋgandàk.
Ɓàsàa ɓa ŋkàl lɛ mùt wı̌m à yèe a tı̄ wɛ̀ bı̀jɛk lı̀ɓit li kahal sòghɛ̀.
Ɓàsàa ı̀ mɓèna ɓe ɓoŋōl lɛ̂y.
Ɓàsaaŋgo nı̀ ɓanyàŋgo ɓa kɛ̂ i dinâ, bı̀saaŋgo bitân.
Ɓàsàhànyik ɓa ntùlul ndigi ikède bikay.
Ɓàsak àsikò ɓa mɓɔ̀ŋ tond.
Ɓàsak bı̀kekeŋ ɓa ntòl ha ɓe pak!
Ɓàsak ndı̀ŋ ɓa ntòl ha ɓee.
Ɓàsaŋ ɓɔŋ ɓana.
Ɓasi i nnimil mɛ ı̄ jɔ̄mbɛ̂.
Ɓàsogol ɓɔn ɓa yı̄glɛ ɓěs màtı̀ŋ ma nı̂ŋ.
Ɓàsɔ ɓa kâgdɛ̀gɛ̀ yàk wɛ̀ ù kàgdɛ̀gɛ̀, ɓa mâl yàk wɛ̀ ù mâl!

Ɓàti ɓa ɓāhlak mbambà.
Ɓàtı̀ı̀ mbɔ̀m isı̄ ɓa njɛ̄ ɓe ntu nugā.
Ɓàtòhtòs ɓa mpam Makàk, ndi ɓàkı̀s ɓa mɓèna kwɔnā ɓɔ!
Ɓatôk à ŋ̀ɔŋ njumb i ŋgı̀i pōndı̂, inyùulɛ̄ bı̀tòŋ bi ye ŋgàndàk, ndi à ntēe gwɔbiso ŋgèlè yàda.
Ɓàtòlɛ̀ ɓa mɓɔgna ŋwı̀i.
Ɓàtòlɛ̀ ɓa ntop lituba matɛ̄bɛ̂l.
Ɓàtòlò ɓa nloŋha mɛ màŋwı̀ı̀ i màtɛbɛ̂l; bı̀lambɛ gwes bi nlōŋhà.
Ɓàtòlò ɓa nlùhlana ɓe i ŋwı̀ı̀.
Ɓàtùk bɔ̂y ɓa ntèdnà.

Ɓàudu ɓa mɓɔk bikààt.
Ɓàudu ɓa mɔhna lɔŋgɛ lɔŋgɛ̂!
Ɓàudu ɓa mpɛ̀hnà i nlòŋ i ŋgèdà màjòp ma ndap sǔglù.
Ɓàudu ɓa mpùm lɛ!
Ɓàudu ɓa nhı̄imbɛ bisonda ŋgɔ̀k.

Ɓàudu ɓa sǔglù ɓa nlamb minsɔ̀mbɔ̀ mi kɔɔ.
Ɓàudu ɓa sûglù ɓa ńyàglà.

Ɓòmb ǹyèe.
Ɓòmbà i malep i tegi mɛ̀ i kède ndāp.
Ɓombo ŋkɔŋ i ŋkahal ɓòŋa nı̀ màŋgɔ̀si dilɔ̄ tini.
Ɓòmbol mɛ̀ mǎn likàbò lı̂.
Ɓòmɓàkòt à ŋgwāl nya ndi nya bı̄ɔmb.
Ɓòmlɛnɛ tɔ̀nɛ̀ nı̀ hamà!
Ɓòmlı̀kòt à m̂mâl mɛ wɔ̌m makɔ̀ndɔ̀!
Ɓòmol mɛ̀ lı̀kòga lini!
Ɓondol têk i ŋkwêl nyɛ kòò.
Ɓoŋɓoŋ mût.
Ɓòŋgo à ǹsomā i ndɔ̀ndɔ̀k.
Ɓòŋgo ɓēgel ŋŋɔ.
Ɓòŋgo màsı̂n nyɛn à yè nyɛ ɓegel ŋŋɔ.
Ɓòŋhana mɛ̀ gwɔ̀m gwɛ̂m.
Ɓoŋnɛ mɛ̀ pàdà lɛ mɛ̀ nlɔ̀ i pōdôs nyɛ.
Ɓòŋòl jàm i ndı̀dı̀.
Ɓòo bɛ̀ɛ̀ bi kakāò i kède ŋ̀kòp.
Ɓòo mɓòŋ i ŋkogà, wɛ̀ɛ dı̀ gaɓāna ɓɔ̂blà!
Ɓòò mût.
Ɓòò njı̂ŋ.
Ɓòò nugā i nhuùmbà.
Ɓòò nugā i nnùmb tûktùk.
Ɓoonɛ i pos i mɓabaa mɛ̂.
Ɓooò! kinjɛ̄ nyà jàm ı̀ni!
Ɓos lı̀kòga.
Ɓòt ɓa biyòy nyɛ.
Ɓòt ɓa ɓā ɓa nhɔ̄ŋlɛ ɓes màm dı̀ biɓɔ̀ŋ.
Ɓòt ɓâ ɓa nteba i kède nân.
Ɓòt ɓa ɓolō ɓa ye ŋgàndàk Edeyà.
Ɓòt ɓa egı̄ ı̄nyùu màhèhŋà ma bitɛl bi anɛ̀.
Ɓòt ɓa hilùga ɓa ŋ́wɔ̄ ɓe nyuu.
Ɓòt ɓa ini lɔ̀ŋ ɓa nsɛ̀mna ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa Jean Bikògoo ɓa nsāk Asikò.
Ɓòt ɓa jɔmɔ̂l ɓa mɓāmnà.
Ɓòt ɓa kwāŋ ɓɔn ɓa ɓe yi kòt mbɛt.
Ɓòt ɓa liɛ̀mb nı̀ ɓòt ɓa ŋgadla ɓa mɓēges likı̀k.
Ɓòt ɓa lɔ̂k i jɛ̄!
Ɓòt ɓa makàŋ ɓa mɓɛ̄na ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa ması̀ŋ ɓa mɓɛ̄hna isı̄.
Ɓòt ɓa ması̀ŋ ɓa ńyàtnà.
Ɓòt ɓa ması̀ŋ ɓa ŋkahal ni ablànà.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓàmblànà.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓēges Hilòlômb hii kɛl.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓèna kâl lɛ pàdà à ǹnyol ɓanɛɛbɛ̀ lı̀ɓòndo.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓèna nɔhɔp hyee i ngèdà hı̀kaŋ.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓèna wɔ likòlòl i ŋwɔ̌m mi sēp.
Ɓòt ɓa m̂ɓɔgi.
Ɓòt ɓa mɓudɓà.
Ɓòt ɓa mindaŋ ɓa ŋāglana ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa mindaŋ ɓa ŋkɛ̀ ɓa ŋāmbnà.
Ɓòt ɓa mmâl wɔ munu mbɔ̄k ı̀ni, yɔ̌m dı̀ ŋgi gweē ndigi kı̀ bı̀ɓum ni bı̀ɓum.
Ɓòt ɓa mɔ̂k ɓa nsol nyɛ; pân yɛ̂m i nsōl liɓòŋgò.
Ɓòt ɓa mɔ̂k ɓa ntēda lɔŋgɛ̂.
Ɓòt ɓa ncagna hɔp.
Ɓòt ɓa ncɛ̄lɛl njâl nı̀ màkɔ̀n dilɔ̄ tini.
Ɓòt ɓa ncı̀m ? ncı̄m ? ngandàk dilɔ̄ tini!
Ɓòt ɓa ndim; ndim ı̀ yè kɔ̀n.
Ɓòt ɓa nhāhla hyaŋgaa i mbēdge!
Ɓòt ɓa nhāŋ ɓe tɔŋna i tı̀.
Ɓòt ɓa nhigis yı̂mb.
Ɓòt ɓa nhı̀m kii i ndāp ɓɔ̀ma?
Ɓòt ɓa njagı̄ ɓa nlɛgna mɔɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa nlāŋ hiɓoy maɔ̀k ŋgèdà ɓa mâl hɔɔ̄ maɔ̀k mɔmasonā.
Ɓòt ɓa nligna bilı̀yà.
Ɓòt ɓa nlɔ ı̄ hı̄ŋı̂l mbɔk.
Ɓòt ɓa nnimil lipàn ɓa mɓēglànà.
Ɓòt ɓa nnɔ̀ndna mbôŋ.
Ɓòt ɓa nnyı̄ip mût kɔ̀n, ɓa nnyiibàk cı̀bi nı̀ hi jâm li mahindi.
Ɓòt ɓa nsàndà.
Ɓòt ɓa nsɔn ɓa nsèblana lɛ sɔlôŋ.
Ɓòt ɓa ntām mɛ̂.
Ɓòt ɓa nyāŋgɓɛnɛ mɛ̂.
Ɓòt ɓa ńyɛɛlɛnɛ ɓes màhɔŋɔ̂l map.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋàk mɛ yàŋgà yàŋgà.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋēŋâ.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋgadla ɓa nlògna ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋgagâl ɓa ŋgwēs ɓe nsàŋ.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋgwēs egı̂ptò ŋ̀kògo ı̀lɔ̀ɔ̀ lı̀kay li ŋkògo.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋkɔ̀n binyɔ̀ɔ̀ wɔ̀ŋi.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋkɔ̀n ǹlèmbà wɔ̀ŋi.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋkùmnà.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋŋɔmbɔk ɓa mɓèna yeēnɛ biɓūŋgâ.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋɔ̄dɔp Nyambɛ màsɔda ma mɓɛ̀mb ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓa ŋɔŋ bilap bikāy inyùu lı̀sɔ̀lɔ̀p jàm.
Ɓòt ɓa wip ɓa njùbul ɓe ŋwɛ̀mɛl.
Ɓòt ɓa wip ɓa nsa nyɛ̄ jùu.
Ɓòt ɓa wip ɓa ńyɛɛlànà.
Ɓòt ɓa yûm ɓa ŋgwèèla minsɔn.
Ɓòt ɓaà ɓa lɔ̀ɔ hana yàni, kı̀kı̀i mɛ̀ gwèe bı̀nàŋ biɓaà, mɛ̀bi là teeda ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓaaâ ɓɔn ɓa nlal lɛ̂n fàa i mbāy dɔ̂ktà.
Ɓòt ɓada.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa mɓèna nidɓa inyùu lı̀yɔt.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa njɛ̄ ɓakòlò.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa njɛ̄ ŋwâŋ.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa ŋāmb nyuu yak mùt ŋgambi.
Ɓòt ɓahɔgi ɓa ŋkàl lɛ lı̀yàl li mɓàhal ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa ŋkɔ̀n miŋkugı̀ wɔ̀ŋi.
Ɓòt ɓàhɔgi ɓa ŋòmbɓɛnɛ inyùu lı̀hat.
Ɓòt ɓanâ.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa biɓāŋnà, ɓa ŋkahal kwɛ̀l ntoŋ.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa biyùmhà.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa mɓān ŋɛm ikède ndèèŋgà yǎp nı̀ njiiyà yǎp.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa mɓɔ̂glana ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa mpùnnà.
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa ŋgwēhna inyǔkı̄i?
Ɓòt ɓana ɓa ŋkahal āŋna diun cap.
Ɓòt ɓay ɓa nlɔ̀.
Ɓòt ɓɔɓaso ɓā mɓegı̂.
Ɓòt ɓɔɓasonā ɓa nlɔ̂.
Ɓòt ɓɔŋ ɓa mpı̄dɓana kı̂yaga.
Ɓòt ɓɔŋ ɓa ńyubdaha ɓɔɓasô.
Ɓòt ɓɔŋ ɓa ŋòòha mɛ ǹlɛŋ i mbāy nân; nyɛ nı̀ ɓòt ɓɛ̂m ɓa ŋòòhà.
Ɓòt jùɛ̀m.
Ɓoy maɔ̀k ma lien.
Ɓɔ ɓâ ɓa nnı̂gha mɛ̂; à ǹnı̂gha mɛ yèl i têblè; dı̀ ǹnı̂gha gwêl.
Ɓɔ mǎn ɓa nhooɓànà.
Ɓɔ mànyâŋ ɓa edı̄ kı̀i lı̀ɓàl ɓɔ ı̀si.
Ɓɔ̀ mùt wɔ̀ŋ halà kiki à mɓòndɛ lɛ̂n i kɛ̄l ŋgànd!
Ɓɔ̀ nyɛ nı̀ ŋ̀koot we ɓɔ̂ŋg, ha kı̀i à ǹlɛ̂glɛ mɛ̂, mɛ̀ ganɔ̄l nduk kii!
Ɓɔ tɛl à ŋ̀wɔ.
Ɓɔ̀blà i ŋkèŋa lɔŋgɛ̂.
Ɓɔblà nı̀ jàm.
Ɓɔ̀bɔ̀ŋ i njɛ̄ hiòndɛ̀.

Ɓɔɓaso ɓa ŋkɛ mintùk.

Ɓɔdà piyà i ye lām ni ɓɔ̀blà.

Ɓɔl hı̀òndɛ̀.
Ɓɔl njɛ̀l.

Ɓɔ̀ma i ɓalêt i mmâl.
Ɓɔ̀ma i ntāgɓɛ i mbēdge sǔglù.

Ɓɔ̀mba pià.
Ɓɔ̀mbɔ i nnɛ̀.
Ɓɔ̀mbɔ yɛn ini?
Ɓɔ̀n ɓa mińyèe ɓa nlɛ̀lna ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.

Ɓɔ̌n ɓa nlɔ̄nd i lı̀gwelel.

Ɓɔ̀n ɓa ŋgwɔ ɓa ŋkahal ānâ.

Ɓɔ̀n ɓa ye ɓàyeglɛ̀ ɓa ɓagwâl ɓap.

Ɓɔ̌n ɓòlom ɓòo, bı̀ɓum ɓòo.

Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋkàlna diŋgàŋganà kòkoa i pāŋ hyèe.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋkɛ̂ jɔ̀gɔ̂p ɓa kahal ndugi kòt maŋgudga.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋkɛ̀ mbumbùhà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋkɛ̀ ŋgwee liɓāy li mintùk.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋkwàdna i kɛ mintùk i mbēdge.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋŋwàhna nsɔn.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋŋwɛ̄hna malep.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋòdnà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋom kɛmbɛ̂ ǹsondo.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋom masɛ̀ɛ nı̀ sǔglù yɔ̀sô.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋōmna ŋgɔ̂k.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋ́wâblana ni ŋgɔ̀k.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ŋ́wàdna gwalâk.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa sûglù ɓa mɓàdna mambàdgà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa sûglù ɓa mɓèna jɛ makàlà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa sǔglù ɓa mɓèna kɔ̂n masulûk i ŋgèdà mbèŋ.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa sûglù ɓa mɓumblɛ malêt wǎp ŋgwee.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa sûglù ɓa njòp ɓuluɓùlù.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa wanda ɓa nhɔ̄mbna miŋɔ.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa wanda ɓana ɓa ntı̂p ɓiinà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ye ı̄ ndɛ̀ŋgɛ̀ɛ̀.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ye ı̄ ndɛ̀ŋgɛ̀l.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa yê ńyı̄ŋa maŋgòlò.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓana ɓa mɓèna ntùk.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓancâŋgɓɛ̄nɛ i ndāp sǔglù.
Ɓɔ̀̀ŋgɛ ɓɛ̂m ɓa ncilà.
Ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓɔn ɓa njò mı̂m dilɔ̄ tunu.
Ɓɔɔ yàgi ù ŋkɔ̀n.
Ɓɔɔga mɛ̀ bı̀holo bi bipos bini.
Ɓɔ̀sogol ɓɔn ɓa yı̄glɛ ɓěs ı̀ni mbāy.
Ɓɔ̀sɔŋ ɓanân.
Ɓɔ̌t à ǹlɔ̂; ɓɔ̀ɓɔ̌t ɓa nlɔ̂; ɓɔ̀t yɛ̂m nunu; ɓɔ̀ɓɔ̀t yɛ̂m ɓa nlɔ̀.
Ɓɔ̀t i nhēnd lâŋlàŋ.
Ɓɔt i ŋɛm yɛ̂m yɔsô i yenɛ̀ i wɛ̀ɛnı̄.
Ɓɔt mùt jàm.
Ɓɔ̀t njaŋgumba.
Ɓɔt ŋ̀ɛm yak Hı̀lòlômb.
Ɓɔ̀t yɛ̂m i ńyɔn lɛ ɓaŋ!
Ɓudɛ mǎn i nàŋ.
Ɓudnɛ mɛ̀ bı̀jɛk gwɛ̂m.
Ɓuga jɔp nyɛn mɛ̀ ŋkɛ̀ mintùk.
Ɓugû yɔ̌m kagaga!
Ɓùhgà màmbɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀.
Ɓuk i lisı̀hı̀.
Ɓuk i lisı̀s.
Ɓuk yɔŋ i mɓabaa mɛ̂.
Ɓùlùs à yè ŋgı̀m ǹsɔ̀ŋgi.
Ɓum ɓacɔ ɓa yɔ̂l.
Ɓùŋgɛ ɓànjɛ̌mjɛ̀ mu ı̄ pɔ̄ɔ̄!
Ɓùp lı̀ɓap à ŋ̀kwɔ̂.
Ɓùp u nsây bieŋa.
Ɓùp u ŋkôn.
Ɓuugɛnɛ màn hês!
Ɓùùnɛ ɓanjɛ̌mjɛ̀ i nsèbla lɛ jǎy.
Câ à kɛmbɛ̂!
Cà mbumbun.
Cagɛ̂ mbahà.
Càhà di nyik di ŋŋom mɛ̂.
Càndi cɛ̂m di ŋògà ɓe kɛlkı̀ikɛ̄l.
Càndi di ŋembâ.
Caŋɛ̀s ı̀ yè ɓohol ɓatɔ̀nɛ̀.
Caŋɛ̀s ı̀ni ı̀ ǹhola mɛ i ɓohôl ɓàtɔ̀nɛ̀ ɓɔɓasô.
Cas nı̄ mɛ̂ lı̀ɓàdò jɔŋ.
Cǎy di ɓêk di mmèles bikèy.
Cǎy di mɓèna hoda ni sēp.
Cày di ńyɔ̀ɔ̀dɛ̀.
Cèè cɔŋ cɔtāma di kolı̄ nı̀ mɛ̀.
Cèè di malɔŋ.
Cèe di ncebâ.
Cèe nı̀ ɓàdak cɔ tı̄ni.
Cèmbi di bitūba; mɔ̀t ma bitūba nyɛ ǹlèlèm hɔma.
Cena ı̄ mɓèna ɓe haŋ i ɓūm makàŋ.
Cɛŋɓɛ̂s à yè lɛ di yɔ̂ŋ njɛ̌l ı̀ni.
Cɛ̀ŋɓɛ̂s jàm.
Cɛ̂p i ńyɔ̂glà.
Cı̂mbɛ̀ i ŋkeda nı̀ ǹsùl.
Còdot di mɓày ɛ̂ŋgɛ̀ŋg.
Còŋ ces di ye dı̀hindi.
Còŋ cɔŋ di ŋkòyòp.
Còŋ di naŋ wɛ̂, kɛ̀ kɔhɔl ŋ̀ŋɔ wɔŋ!
Còŋ di ńyɛ̀ɛ̀mbɛnɛ nyɛ lɛtɛ̀ɛ̀ nı̀ i mbūs.
Còs cɔtāma di ɓāk lɛ di nɔl nyɛ.
Còs di nhol nyɛ i sū.
Còs di nnyāŋâ.
Cǒs di nnyēŋel mɛ ı̄ mbūs.
Cɔ u ye ndùdù.
Cɔ̀bi cɔdisô, dı̀nùni cɔdisô.
Cɔ̀bi di njɛ̄ ɓanyɛ̀gi.
Cɔ̀bi di nloba ŋgandàk.
Cɔ̀bi di ŋoga ŋgandàk.
Cɔ̀glaga di hyɔbı̄ di ŋkòyòp.
Cɔlop i maŋgɛ.
Cugul mɛ̀ bı̀tòŋ gwɛ̂m bini.
Cugul mɛ̀ bı̀tòŋ i ncɔ̄bɔ.

Di êdha hyèe mu māsǎgā ma ye ı̄ wɔ̌m.
Di kɛ dı̄ jôp miŋkɔ̀ŋ mi ye ǹlědhàk nı̀ dı̀kòya.
Di kobda hêmlɛ̀ mɔ̀ɔ.
Di m̂ɓohla i Kàya.
Di ǹhôgha; à ǹhogha mɛ ŋgı̀m ŋgɛŋ yadā lɛ̂n.
Di ŋ́wàɛnɛ ŋgôy ɓàkwɛ̀dɛ̀.
Dilɔ̄ tini ɓa mɓēmbes ɓôt mɔ̀ɔ.
Dipùma tini di nhoolàhà.
Dı̀ bi ēmbha candi, ndi nyɛ à ma jɛ̄ nlom sō mû!
Dı̀ bi hàbnɛ ŋganda.

Dı̀ ɓak i ntɔa pooga i kòdòk.
Dı̀ ɓak i pèmsan nyɔ̀gi, mɛ̀ ɓum nyɛ.

Dı̀ ɓe kɛ ɓǎŋ njèe ı̀ tihil ɓes bisū.
Dı̀ ebha màlep i Kàya i ŋgèdà lı̀ɓii jɔ̄ŋ.

Dı̀ɔ̀ksàp di tee lı̄pàn jɛ̂m.
Dı̀pek di kiŋ.
Dı̀pɔ̀s di masoo.
Dı̀pùma dı̀kɛŋi cɔdisô di ntolâ.
Dı̀san di mbɔk di ntùlul ɓambɔmbɔ̀k.
Dı̀sɔ̀n di nsàndà.
Dı̀sɔ̀n di ŋɔ̀ŋ munu maɓāp ma ndap.
Dı̀sùhù di mpam nyɛ kı̀i à ǹtɛhɛ mı̂m; dı̀sùhù di ŋkop nyɛ!
Dı̀tàtàŋgà di ntòl i ndèè sèp.
Dı̀ùmbà di nnɛ̄nɛ ŋgı̂m makèk.
Dı̀ǔnà di mpùùɛ vururu.
Dı̀yàna cɔ̄ŋ di nhōla ɓe mɛ tɔ̀ jàm.
Dɔkêt li ntɔŋ ɓodàa li nnɛɛbànà.
Dɔktà à m̂ɓeelaha mɛ mı̌s.
Dɔ̂ktà à mɓōblɛnɛ nyɛ i kɔ̀sɛ̀.
Dɔ̂kta à mɓōblɛnɛ nyɛ i ndāp màtibla.
Dɔ̂ktà à ǹhɔɔ mɛ fāyà i pɔ̄ɔ.

Dɔ̂ktà à ǹtabal ŋkɔ̀kɔ̂n.
Dɔ̂ktà à ǹti mɛ bɛ̀ɛ bi minsɔŋ.

Hɔ̀hlɛnɛ màŋgɛ jɔmb lini!
Hɔl bı̀taŋlɛnɛ gwɔŋ bi maŋgà.
Hɔ̀ma bı̀tèk nunu à ǹlama ɓûmblànà.
Hɔ̀ma gwèt bi yê lı̀kàt li ŋgwɛ̀l ɓôt.
Hɔ̀ma nunu à ye ɓɛ̀ɛ̀m.
Hɔ̀ma nyùu à ŋ̀kiı̂.
Hɔ̀ma ŋgàdà.
Hɔmb mɛ̀ bı̀ɓam gwɛ̂m.
Hɔmb ŋ̀ɔ.
Hɔn jâm!
Hɔn kilâ mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ̂ !
Hɔ̀n lep.
Hɔ̀ŋgɔ̀ɔ̀ nyɛ̀mb.
Hɔŋlɛ ini mɛ̀ m̂ɓiinɛ wɛ̂.
Hɔŋɔl ɓɔ̀ŋ man bɛ̀ɛ̀ bi jos.
Hɔɔ kèbel mɛ̂.
Hɔɔ mùt yàŋ.
Hɔ̀ɔ̀hà jɔ̌mb ? hɔ̀ɔ̀hà jɔmb ?
Hɔɔmbà mût.
Hɔɔmbɛ̀ hı̀ɓɛ̀ɛ.
Hɔɔndɛ̀ hı̀ɓɛ̀ɛ.
Hɔɔŋgɛ̀ mùt.
Hɔp mbâŋ; Yesù Krı̌stò à ɓe podhɛ̀nɛ̀ màmùt i mbàŋ.
Hɔp mɛ̀ ǹnyuŋul lı̀ɓê wɔn u ye lɛ̄ ɓàsàa.
Hɔp u ɓasàa u nhāŋ ɓe ni ŋgèni.
Hɔp u ɓasàa u nlɛ̀t.
Hɔp u ɓayi jàm u nnɔ̀m ɓee.
Hɔp u segi.
Hɔp û u nhyamɓaga haàmm, ǹlom a kwɔ̂ ŋkāa.
Hɔp we u ye ŋgı̀ podâ.
Hɔp wɔŋ u mpuūaha hikwàa.
Hɔp wɔŋ u ŋkwèla lɛ̂n.
Hɔp wɔŋ u ŋūnɓaha mɛ̂.
Hɔsı̀ i ŋkɛ̀ ŋgwee ŋgandàk.
Hɔsı̀ ı̀ ŋkɔ̀n titiı̄ yee wɔ̀ŋi.
Hɔsı̀ ı̀ ŋkɔ̀n titı̂ ye wɔ̀ŋi.
Hɔ̀y i gweē mɛ̀.
Hɔ̀ya ŋŋɛm.
Hubûs u joy.
Hudɓaha mɛ̀ mbɔt yɛ̂m ɓòlo.
Hudɛ ŋ̀ŋɔ.
Hudlaha nyɛ̄ ŋ̀kòò ū; ɓa nhudlaha miŋkòò.
Hudlɛnɛ mɛ̀ ɓàtɔ̀nɛ̀.
Hùgà jɔmb.
Hùgà ŋkɔ̀k.
Hùgɓɛ̀ i ye hāna liɓɛ̀bi: hɔ̀ma hùgɓɛ̀.
Hùgdɛ̀ ŋgɔ̀nd i ŋgɔ̀k.
Hùglɛ̀ i mbɛbı̄
Hugûl kop macɛ̀ɛ.
Hùhlàgà à ŋ̀kɔgɔ̄ɔ nyɛ.
Huhul i nlek hyee.
Huluk ŋɛm!
Hùlul bijɛ̄k bi nholôl.
Hùlùl jàm.
Hulul mɛ̀ ɓàk.
Hulul nyɛ m̂pı̀ŋga, lı̀hɛp li ta ɓee.
Hùlùù màkàbò; hùlùù bı̀tèk.
Hund bı̀nan.
Hundha nyɛ̄ bı̀nan; nı̀ ǹlama hundha bini bı̀nan.
Hùndùl à ǹtagɓɛ̀.
Hundul binan.
Hundul mɛ̀ bı̀nan.
Hùt mùt.
Huu ɓūŋga yɔ̄ŋ, u naŋāl!
Huu mbāy yɔ̂ŋ.
Huû ŋgààŋgò.
Hùùbɛ̀ i ye hāna liɓɛ̀bi li mbegde.
Huudɛ̀ kɛ̀y.
Huuhà mùt i mbāy yeē.
Hùùlɛ yɛ̂m i mpût kı̀.
Hùùlɛnɛ mɛ̀ m̂ɓòŋ.
Huunɛ mɛ̀ hyèe.
Hùùrù ɓakɔ̄ŋ!
Hùùrù jê!
Huyɛ sàho, hyɔ̀bi.
Hyǎk hi kɛmbɛ̂; ɓepkɛmbɛ̂ ɓa bihèa jak i yeglɛ i nnāŋ nsɔ.
Hyàmàmi hi ntèèŋga mɛ hāna i kɛ̀y.
Hyandâl mùt nı̀ kek.
Hyàndi hi mpà; à ŋ̀gwiyā i hyàndi hyɔŋ.
Hyàndi hyee; ı̀ hyee.
Hyàŋ hi njɔ̂k.
Hyǎŋ hi njɔ̂k.
Hyàŋgaa hi mɓày.
Hyàŋgaa hi mɓày ɓaàm.
Hyàŋgaa hi mɓeē mɛ lɛ̀n ŋgı̀m kɛl.
Hyàŋgaa hi mɓèyes soŋ.
Hyàŋgaa hi mɓèyey mbɔt.
Hyàŋgaa hi nhɔ̄ɔ yeha kɛl.
Hyàŋgaa hi nnyāy.
Hyàŋgaa hi ntembes malep.
Hyàŋgaa hi ńyambà.
Hyàp njêk.
Hyǎs? hyas? hyàs? hi mbay.
Hyas mùt.
Hyǎy hi ɛ.
Hyày hi likɔ̀ndɔ̀ hi ŋ́wândlà; ŋgàŋgò yɔ̀ŋ ı̀ ŋ́wàndlà ɓe.
Hyǎy hi nlɛ̄ŋɛl malēp.
Hyǎy hi nlɛŋɛp malēp.
Hyǎy hini hi ŋkɔyı̂.
Hyèdel lı̀pɔ̀ndɔ hana i mɛ̌nı̄.
Hyèè hi jala.
Hyèe hi ncedà.
Hyèe hi ncêl limâ.
Hyèe hi nlēk liklik.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ ɓûp ɓùp.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ ɓuùmm.
Hyèe hi nlɔŋ hi siyɛ̂; siyɛ mùt nunu lɔ̄ŋgɛ̂.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ mpàmbi.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ ndɔŋ ndɔŋ.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ; ŋwày u nlɔ̄ŋ.
Hyèe hi nlɔ̄ŋ tɔ̂ŋtɔ̀ŋ.
Hyèe hi nsiynɛ nyɛ mbɔt i ndāp.
Hyèe hi ntɔ̀ŋɓɛ̀.
Hyèe hi ŋkaàmbà.
Hyèe hi ŋkalà.
Hyèe hi ye cèdel yɛ̂m makalâk.
Hyèe hini hi mpām njanjàt.
Hyèe hyɔn nūnu mùt à yè!
Hyèlel mɛ̀ màmbɔt mɛ̂m.
Hyèlel yɛ̂m i makàlà i ye hɛ̄ɛ?
Hyèmbi hyes; ı̀ hyes hini.
Hyɛ̀ɛ̀ hi hyɔbı̄ hi nnɔ̄hɔp hyaŋgaa.
Hyɛ̌l màtoà nyɔ̀nɔ!
Hyɛ̀lɓa lɛ̄ mɛ ɓɛ̄ŋgɛ lɔŋgɛ yɔŋ mbɔt.
Hyı̀bi hi tolɛ̀ hini!
Hyı̀da hı̄ nsòghɛ mı̌s.
Hyı̀i hi nsulūl mɛ̂.
Hyòbi hi ŋkɛ̀ lɛŋgɛlɛ̀ŋgɛ̀.
Hyòɓôt hi ŋgwɛ̂l ŋkwaŋ.
Hyolol yɔŋ i ye hɛ̄ɛ?
Hyomnà mùdàa.
Hyòo hi ńyɔ̂ŋ man kōp.
Hyòò hi pondol hi hɔ̄ɔ ŋgandàk.
Hyǒp hyɔn ɓa mɓèna sal hana i ɓěhnı̄.
Hyôt wip.
Hyɔ̀bi hi mpɛ̄ghɛ linjɛŋgɛ.
Hyɔ̀bi hi njɛ̄ ǹlɔp kɛ̀bkɛ̀p.
Hyɔ̀bi hi njôp cǎt i kède lēp.
Hyɔ̀bi hi ŋkoma hi ŋkɛ̀ bisèsèni.
Hyɔ̀bi hyada.
Hyɔ̀bi hyɔ̂k hi nnɛ̀.
Hyɔ̀bi hyɔmɛ̀dɛ hı̂.
Hyɔ̀bi hyɔn mɛ̀ ǹjɛ.
Hyɔ̀bi yomi.
Hyɔlɛ̀ i ye mɛ̀ ɓègel i ɓɔn ɓa gwɔm ɓa mahindi.
Hyɔlɛ̀ yɛ̂m i ye nı̀ ɓàŋguŋâ.
Hyɔ̀mɔm hi ntèèŋga ɓes!
Hyɔ̀nɔn hi ŋkɔ̀n nyɛ.
Hyɔ̀ɔ̂n hi nsulūl mɛ̂.
Hyɔ̂p hyǒp.
Hyù hi nnɛ̀ nsūgi ŋgandàk!
I bı̀hègel bi mbɔk - bihègel bi mbɔk.
I ɓa ɓe wɛ̂ dı̀ nlà ɓe kôs tɔhı̂.
I ɓā lɛ̄ ù ǹsaâ ɓe mɛ̂, mɛ̀ nsɔ̄man wɛ̂.
I ɓā nı̄ lɛ à ǹnyagal nyɔ̂ ndi à pɔt, à ŋ́wɔ̄.
I ɓɛ̌t ɓa gweē ŋgùy, ɓa kɛnɛ̄k ŋ̀gwee.
I ɓòlo ini i mmelēs mɛ ɓı̀ı̀bɛ̀.
I ɓòmm nû, mɛ̀ ǹnɔk ndigi mùdàa à ŋ̀ɔŋ nlend!
I ɓòt ɓâ.
I ɓòt ɓa nnibil wɛ̂, ɓa ye ɓàlɛŋɛ̂l jùu.
I ɓòt ɓɛ̂m ɓâ!
I ɓòt ɓɔŋ ɓâ ɓa nsāanà ɓee.
I hɛ̌t mɛ̀ yè, à yè lɔŋgɛ̂!
I hɔ̀ma lēp nunu à ńyɔ̀ŋà.
I hɔ̀ma mànyùgnà ma yê wı̌p u nhāŋ ɓe hâ.
I hɔ̀ma nunu à yè wɛ̀m.
I hɔ̀ma nunu; i mùt nunu à nibil mɛ̀ bı̀jɛk; i ndāp.
I jòy li Isāŋ, nı̀ li Man nı̀ li Mbuu M̀pubi, àmɛ̀n! tɔ̀ lɛ «i jǒy li Tatà, nı̀ li Man nı̀ li Mbuu M̀pubi, àmɛ̀n!».
I kà ı̀ yè lɛ.
I kààt ı̀ni ı̀ gwèe ndı̀mbhɛ̀ màm ù m̂ɓât mɛ̂.
I kède màmbɔt manâ mɛ̀ ǹsabā yadā.
I kɛ̄l ɓa mɓɛ̀l ŋɔ mût i mbāy ŋgeŋgê, ɓa mpɔ̄t lɛ kàà à ŋ̀kɔ̂p maɓòŋ ŋgê.
I kɛ̄l lı̀ɓiı̂ dinâ li nhāŋ ɓēe.
I kı̄ŋ nyɛn à bisùmul mɛ̂ ŋ̀kòò.
I kɔ̀sɛ̀ mɛ̀ mɓèna ɓa i têblè, ndi i kɔ̀sɛ̀ jùu mɛ̀ mɓèna ɓa i nàŋ.
I lèman nyɛn mɛ̀ mɓèŋgɓànà.
I lɛ̌n ı̀ni ndèk ɓɔn ɓa mbɛnɛ yɔ̄n i ŋgi sak lı̀hoŋgo.
I lɔ̀ŋ ɓasàa lı̀sɔ̀ mɔ̀ɔ li mûnlom li nlɛ̄l ɓe dilɔ ditân, li mudàa kı̂ dı̀lɔ dinâ.
I Maɓǒŋ-lɔ̀ŋ.
I màŋgɛ nunu à ndɔ̄gɔp lɛ!
I màŋgɛ nunu à nnòlhà; ɓa nôlhà.
I mbāy yês ɓòt ɓa mpāla ɓe naŋàl.
I mbāy yɔ̂ŋ nyɛn à ŋɔ̄ŋɓɛ̀nɛ̀, ndi hana ɓe.
I mbɔ̀mbɔ̂m hı̀kòa.
I mbūs jɔ̀gɔ̂p, mɛ̀ nsàhɓa malep.
I mbūs ŋ̀kɔ̀là mɛ̀ ŋ̀kôhlɛ̄ môŋ inyùu kùynɛ̀ hyèe i kı̄isı̀n.
I mɓèda mɛ mɔ̀ni.
I mmâl ɓahàɓa.
I mpōp puum.
I mùdàà nû kinjɛ̄ɛ kɔ̄yɔ̂p ini!
I mùt à m̂ɓada mɛ̂ màpɛp a yihā mɔ̄.
I mùt nunu à gwèe lı̀kus i mbūs.
I mùt nunu à yè lı̀mugɛ̀.
I mùt nuu à mpɔ̄t ɓē, à yè pı̀i.
I mùt nuu à ŋgi yiı̄ ǹsùdà.
I ndè mbɛɛ ɓa bikwèe wɛ̂?
I ndèdà kwàŋ ɓòdàa ɓa ɓe pɔt ɓē mbɔk.
I ndèè ı̀mbɛɛ ɓa neŋel nyɛ?
I ndèe kwàŋ ɓàsogol ɓa ɓênà ɓe mbɔt kı̀i lɛ̀n.
I ndèe mbǎm ùm ı̀ mɓām i hɔ̀ma ɓòt ɓa yê ndi mùt à sɛ̂hlà, wɛ̀ɛ à gwèe hı̀kòm.
I nı̀ŋ ini i ye ɓɛ̄ŋɛ̂l.
I nɔ̀p nunu à yè nı̀ màtanga.
I nsòmbla ɓes bı̀kut bitân inyùu pala sùha têk.
I nsòmbla lɛ ɓa kebēl wɛ̀ ı̀ gwɔŋ bijɛk.
I nsòmbla mɛ ɓālas munu i mbɔ̄t ı̀ni.
I ŋɛ̄m u njeŋ njeŋ.
I ŋgàŋgàŋ jı̌bɛ̀ nyɛn bı̀ɓeba bi mâm bi mɓòŋà.
I ŋgèdà cɔ u mmâl dı̀ mɓèna lɛp bikàgaŋ.
I ŋgèdà kwàŋ ɓa ɓe sɔ̂n ɓɔ̌n lɛ ɓa sèhba ɓâŋ.
I ŋgèdà kwàŋ ɓa ɓe têŋ ɓòdàà i kàdɛ̂ inyùu ŋ̀òŋ.
I ŋgèdà màjònâ ɓòt ɓa ŋŋɛ̀ɛ̀ ŋgandàk.
I ŋgèdà njoyâ u nsāŋ nɔ̌p à nɔ ŋgàndàk.
I ŋgèdà nɔ̌p à ǹnol wɛ̂ ndi u jôp ndāp, ù ŋɛ̀ŋglà, u haba gwɔ̌m bı̀pɛ.
I ŋgèdà sèp mı̀nsàya mi mɓèna ɓe ɓana malep.
I ŋgèdà ù m̂pulɛ gwâl ù mpāla tɛhɛ ɓalàl.
I ŋgèdà ù ǹlɛ̂ŋ ŋgɔ̂k i lēp u temı̄ ù ntɛ̄hɛ mindɔŋ mi ŋkɛ̀ i ŋgı̀ı̀ malep.
I ŋgı̀i ŋ̀ɔ.
I ŋgòy ɓa nsòmbol nɔl ı̀ mpı̀ghà.
I ŋkèla lɛ ŋgê à yè bı̀hès bi ɓôt.
I ŋkèla lɛ ù yè pɛlɛs.
I ŋkɛ̀ laa?
I ŋwɛ̌t à ǹnip mɛ̂ mbɔt a tı̄mbis.
I sōŋ bı̀òôm nyɛn nɔ̌p à nnɔ̄ juū nı̀ binjǎŋmùha.
I sū nyɛn à m̂ɓɔdɓana moo.
I sū nyɛn à ǹtɔnɓana liɓu.
I ta ɓē lɔŋgɛ ı̄ ɓèbɛ̀ ɓòt màm.
I ta ɓē lɔŋgɛ ı̄ ɓòŋòl lɛ̀mb i ŋûn.
I ta ɓē lɔŋgɛ ı̄ pām ɓɛ̀bɛ̀ɛ̀ nı̀ nyǎŋ lɔ̀m.
I ū unu tɔ̀ hyòdot hi nɛnɛ ɓēe.
I yaŋan kɛmbɛ̂.
I ye lɔŋgɛ̂ mɛ̀ wɔ, ı̀ lɔ̀ɔ̀ lɛ mɛ̀ ɓɔ̂ŋ i jàm lı̂.
I ye mɛ̀ lɔŋgɛ̂ mɛ̀ wɔ ı̀lɔ̀ɔ̀ lɛ mɛ̀ kɛ ı̄ jɔ̀mɔ̂l nı̀ mǎntàtâ.
I ye ndèk sı̀ı̂ kı̀i yàlâk.
Iɓālɛ̄ à ńyı̄ jâm à nyahla ɓâŋ.
Iɓālɛ̄ i nsômblā halà.
Iɓālɛ̄ mùt à ŋgwēm ndoŋ ndi hı̀see, ŋ̀kwaha, ŋ̀kòt nyɔɔ u nolâ, tɔ̀lɛ ɓa adal nsɔ̀mbɔ̀ kɔɔ, wɛ̀ɛ mùt nu à m̂pop; ndi iɓālɛ̄ nùga i nhyōm juū yɔn i nnolâ, wɛ̀ɛ mùt à ŋ̀kwɔ ŋkaa.
Iɓālɛ̄ mùt à sòmblak jâm ndi à nyɛgɓa ndigi à m̂ɓana jɔ, wɛ̀ɛ à «m̂bɔmɔ̄p mbɔ̂m tòlɛ̀», inyùulɛ̄ à ŋ̀kôs jâm hɛ̀ ǹsɔn ɓe lɛ à ǹsal..
Iɓālɛ̄ ù ǹlɛ̂ŋ pos i hyèe i ntōm.
Iɓālɛ̄ ù ǹsɛ̂t mɛ̀ nsɛ̀dɛl wɛ̂.
Iɓālɛ̄ ù nsūl ɓe nsɔ̄ŋ, ù ŋɔ̀gɓà.
Iɓālɛ̄ ù ŋ̀gwal ɓɔn wɛ̀ɛ ù m̂ɓɔ̂t.
Iikı̄! Nùna kı̀ mòò ma ŋkoba ni ǹlɔŋ wɔnsô!
Ikède lòk Saŋgo Prɛ̀sbı̀terı̀ɛ̀n ɓa ye ŋ̀kùm wada.
Ikède ǹsɔn matı̀là.
In kɛmbɛ̂, in kop, in ŋgôy.
Îni à nhōmbol hiɓèmà hi nyik bı̀kùlɛ.
Îni à ǹlamb ɓaɔ̀mbɛ̀.
Îni à nsı̀t ndap.
Îni à ǹti mɛ lı̀ɓòk li nlēk.
Îni à ǹyiglɛ ɓe mɛ bı̀jɛk ɛ?
Îni à ŋ̀kit ncà i wɔ̌m.
Ini kègsɛ̀ i ɓāk nyɛ m̂ɓadgà!
Ini nàŋ i ye tidigi.
Ini sāŋgo i bijēl yàŋan ŋgɔ̂nd.
Ini sùgùù i nnɔ̄lâ.
Ini sūlûk i ye ɓàŋgàŋgàà.
Ini tòdò i njēba ni m̂ɓòŋ.
Ini tòŋ i mɓūugà.
Ini tòtò i njēba ni m̂ɓòŋ.
Ini yɔ̀m lɛ ɓùp hı̀uu i ńyı̄ba ha ɓe i pɛ̀s yes mbɔk.
Ini yɔ̀m yɔn mɛ̀ nsèndel ɓaɛ̀mb.
Inı̄ à koblak makɔ̀ndɔ̀ ndi à ɓep maŋgɛ m̂ɓèbi i wɔ̀ɔ.
Inı̄ à mɓàa nsugi.
Inı̄ à m̂ɓegēl mɛ mɛ̂m màsoo.
Inı̄ à mmɛ̀mlɛ ŋkeŋee man.
Inı̄ à ǹnây hiɓɛ̀ɛ̀ hi ŋkono ni cày di makɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Inı̄ à ǹyiglɛ ɓe mɛ bı̀jɛk ɛ?
Inı̄ à ŋāŋ makɔ̀ndɔ̀ ma nyuŋgā.
Inı̄ wês; ɓɔ̀inı̄ ɓes.
Inyǔkı̄ ù ŋkɛ̀ ɓe i sǔglù ? Inyǔlɛ̄ mɛ̀ ŋkɔ̀n.
Inyǔkı̄i à m̂ɓaabɛnɛ i kòò?
Inyǔkı̄i à ǹtolol ɓes mǎŋgòlò?
Inyǔkı̄i ǹsɔŋ à ǹyegēl sa?
Inyǔkı̄i Nyambɛ à hègel mùt?
Inyǔkı̄i ŋgwɔ ı̀ mɓūhûl?
Inyǔkı̄i ù mɓōgɓana mɛ̂?
Inyǔkı̄i ù m̂ɓulɓɛ̀nɛ̀?
Inyǔkı̄i ù ǹhandap njɛ̀l? Ɛ i nhandap ŋkɔ̄ŋ ması̂n.
Inyǔkı̄i ù nhēnel mɛ sàŋ?
Inyǔkı̄i ù nhɔ̄mb ɓana ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ?
Inyǔkı̄i ù ǹloō ɓe hana?
Inyǔkı̄i ù ǹnip isɔ̄ŋ mɔ̀ni?
Inyǔkı̄i ù ńyɔ̄bɓa halà?

Lı̀ɓùùk jɔŋ li kop li ŋkı̀ha ɓe yɔ hàà nı̀ hı̀òndɛ̀.
Lı̀ɓuumbàgà jee li ye kı̀i li mût njèk.
Lı̀ɓuy li ńyèe.
Lı̀cabâk li cee li mûnlom.
Lı̀càdàk jɔŋ li makalâk li nlēm hyee.
Lı̀cagâk li ndêŋg; lı̀cagâk li kuŋgā.
Lı̀càmàk li ŋgân nyɛ̀mb.
Lı̀caŋ li malep.
Lı̀cebel jes li cee lini.
Lı̀cegel li moŋgō lini.
Lı̀cek li bitòdò.
Lı̀cɛ̀ɛ̀ li ɓâs; hı̀ket hi ɓâs; wɔ̀ɔ̀ ɓâs; lı̀nɛ̀ li ɓâs; ntɛ̀t ɓâs.
Lı̀cɛ̀ɛ li ye ùŋgul i hı̀nùni.
Lı̀dùbà li ye lɔ̄ŋgɛ i kède njààŋgò.
Lı̀ebgà jɔŋ li jâm li ye ɓàŋga.
Lı̀èdèk li kɛ̂y li ta ɓē li ɓɛndɛ.
Lı̀en jɔŋ li ŋkandàp ni!
Lı̀en li ŋgwēynɛ i kède wɔ̌m.
Lı̀en li ŋkûdlà.
Lı̀en lini li nlama ɓogà.
Lı̀en lini li ŋàp ŋgandàk!
Lı̀en lini li ye m̂ɓoŋgo ŋgandàk!
Lı̀en mɛ̀ biɓɛ̀l li ŋɔ̂.
Lı̀ènèl ɓòt li ntɔ̀mb ɓee.
Lı̀ɛbɛ̂k jɔŋ li ɓɔŋgɛ tɔ̀ li mimaŋ mi ɓôt li ye lı̀lam.
Lı̀ɛ̀ɛ̀k li mût màɔ̀k li nlɔ̀ɔ̀ hihègà.
Lı̀ɛ̀gɓàk li mût wı̌p.
Lı̀ɛglàk màlep màsuni ma ɛgɛl nyɛ màsɔ̀ŋ.
Lı̀ɛ̀nd li telà li mɓugı̂.
Lı̀ɛ̀nd ŋ̀ɔ li ye ŋgı̀m ɓòlo.
Lı̀gwàndà li nnuŋgi.
Lı̀gweenɛ li Yesù lɛ Yùdeà.
Lı̀gwɛ̀ li makɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Lı̀ha jı̀s li mbâs.
Lı̀ha màkàbò.
Lı̀ha mùt mbàndà.
Lı̀hàà jes li gweē mbɔmbɔ̀k.
Lı̀hàà jɛ̂m li ye lı̀kɛŋi.
Lı̀habgà jee li ta ɓē lilam.
Lı̀hàhà li tôŋ.
Lı̀hâk li ŋkòmɛ̀ i lēp li ta ɓe lilam.
Lı̀hala li nlòòha gwes miŋgɔndɔ.
Lı̀hàn li mɓāhlɛ ki wɛ̂!
Lı̀haŋ li nyik.
Lı̀hee li ŋgôy.
Lı̀hegêk li jɛgi lɛ ɓòdàa ɓa ŋɔ̄k li ntı̄bil gwɛ̂l malep.
Lı̀hègel li kakaò.
Lı̀hel li ŋkòmɛ̀ lini i lēp.
Lı̀hembêk jɔŋ li ŋwɛmɛ̄l li ntèŋga ɓôt.
Lı̀hemel li ŋgɔmbı̄ li ye ı̄ hɛ̌t màtuba ma yenɛ̀; lı̀hemel li dilèlà lini!
Lı̀hɛlɛ̂k mùt à ǹhɛ̂l i ŋgèdà ndùdù.
Lı̀hɛmɛ̂k li ŋɔ ması̂ŋ li nlɔ̄ŋa mao.
Lı̀hɛp jɔn li nnōhɓaha mɛ hyèe.
Lı̀hɛp jɔn li ńyùùɓaha mɛ̂.
Lı̀hɛp li mpēmes nyɛ ɓı̀ı̀bɛ̀.
Lı̀hɛp li nsèyha; ɓànyɔ màɔ̀k ɓa nsèyhà.
Lı̀hɛp li tèèŋgaga mɛ̂, màjò à m̂ɓɔ̂ŋ mɛ m̂ɓùma.
Lı̀hɛp li ye i kɛ̂glà ini.
Lı̀hɛp li ye mɛ̀ ɓòk nı̀ nyùu.
Lı̀hɛ̀yɛ̀k jɔŋ li baàm.
Lı̀himbil li ŋwɛmɛl li ye ndı̄gi jāda.
Lı̀hindi li mbɔmbɔ̀ li kònha wɔŋi.
Lı̀ho li ŋgwɛ̂l liwanda jɛ̂m à ǹnı̂dɓa mɛ̂.
Lı̀hobgà li ŋgaŋgò i ŋgèdà sèp.
Lı̀hodɓàk mbɛbi ı̀ ǹhot biɛ li ŋkēŋ ɓe gwɔ i nāŋ.
Lı̀hodôk ù ǹhot kɛ̀y ini li nlà ɓok yɔ.
Lı̀hôk ù nhō ɓaɓɔ̀ŋ biɓeba bi mâm li nlēmel ɓe lôk ŋgɔmı̂n.
Lı̀holôs lɔ̀ŋ li mɓèŋgɛ ɓôt ɓɔɓasô.
Lı̀hɔgɔ̂k ù nhɔ̄k ni mbūs li nlēmel mɛ̂.
Lı̀hɔŋ li ŋgôy.
Lı̀hɔŋ li ŋgôy li ntɔ̄k mɛ̂.
Lı̀hɔɔ li makòò li ye nyɛ̄.
Lı̀hùdùl kɛmbɛ̂.
Lı̀hùhùgà li nnyɔ̄dnɛ i ɓɔ̀t ndi li kɔ̂gàgà.
Lı̀hus li mpām ŋkɔ̀kɔ̂n nunu i nyɔ̀.
Lı̀hus li sɔbɛ̂; ɓı̀ı̀bɛ̀ i hɔsı̀ i ye lı̀hus.
Lı̀hyàà lı̀ɓɔ̀ɔ lı̀ kùunjà!
Lı̀hyolôl li mɓūm ɓoòlom ɓàpɛ.
Lı̀hyɔl li mɓūm ɓoòlom ɓàpɛ.
Lı̀hyɔ̂l màndap.
Lı̀hyɔl ndāp li ŋŋwemha mɛ màlep i sı̄; dı̀ ŋ̀ŋwemha malep i sı̄.
Lı̀hyɔlɔ̂k jɔŋ li ndap li mpūbus yɔ ŋgàndàk!
Lı̀jês lɔ̀ŋ li nlɔ̀na bisày.
Lı̀jɛ̂k li koŋgo li ŋòbos bijɛk.
Lı̀jɛndɛ li mpàŋ.
Lı̀jòbòk jɔŋ i màm li ŋ́wēha nyuu.
Lı̀jǒl li ɓa omnà bı̀kut; lı̀jǒl li gwêt li ńyɔn ni mı̀m.
Lı̀jɔ̀k li nuga i hyàndi.
Lı̀jùbul li ndap lini.
Lı̀kaa li nnɔ̄l ɓɔn.
Lı̀kaâk jɔŋ li ŋēba lɛ ù yè bı̀tɛmbɛɛ.
Lı̀kàbàk jɔŋ li bijɛk li nnùnda lɛ ù nlà jɛ.
Lı̀kabdà bı̀ɛ li ntùga ɓe koy i kwɔ̀.
Lı̀kàbnà ŋkùs u mût nyɛ ŋgı̀ wɔ li nlɔ̀na liɓua.
Lı̀kàbò li ŋkɔ̂ŋg.
Lı̀kàdàk li ŋkɔ̀ŋ.
Lı̀kàdàk ù ŋ̀kât yaŋan kɛmbɛ̂ ù ɓak lɛ ù ǹnɔl yɔ.
Lı̀kàhɓàk jɔŋ i mbus yɛ̂m li ta ɓe lilam.
Lı̀kàhlàk li soya ŋgı̀ı̀ bikààt.
Lı̀kala li kop.
Lı̀kàmàk ù ŋkàm ɓacàcàŋg li gahı̄gɛ wɛ̂.

Lı̀kap bɔ̂y.

Lı̀kap mǎn.
Lı̀kat li ɓandèèŋgà.

Lı̀kè li ŋkɛ̀kɛ̂.

Lı̀kɛdɛ̂k jɔŋ li bitòdò.

Lı̀kɛ̀nɛ̀k jɔŋ i màm li nsàgal wɛ nı̀ ɓòt.

Lı̀kɛ̀ŋɓàgà jee li ŋŋɔ li ŋkòndɛ ɓebes nyɛ.
Lı̀kidı̂k li ncamā ni lɔ̀ŋ.

Lı̀kı̀nda li yôy.
Lı̀kı̀ŋ li mbɛbı̄ li mɓēdes binan.
Lı̀kobôl màkɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Lı̀kòdòk jɔŋ li hilùŋ li ta ɓē kı̀i jāp.

Lı̀kòga li biɓōha yani.

Lı̀kògi li gweè màòŋg kı̀i mòŋgo.

Lı̀kòndɛ̀ ɓòt mbɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀.
Lı̀kondo li mintaŋ.
Lı̀kondo li nsâglà.
Lı̀kot jee li mɓɔ̀ŋ lɛ à pam ɓe i tı̀ ɓôt.

Lı̀kɔk li njê li ŋgwɛ̂l ntomba.

Lı̀kɔ̀lɔ̀k jɔŋ li bitòŋ li nnı̄mis sɔl ni bı̀kay.
Lı̀kɔ̀mb jɔŋ li ńyòl li nsɔ̀ɔ̀.
Lı̀kɔ̀mb màsù, lı̀kɔ̀mb cǒs.
Lı̀kɔ̀nd li ŋŋwēges nyɛ.
Lı̀kɔ̀nd li ye lɔ̄ŋgɛ ı̄ ŋgedà ikède nı̀ŋ i mût.
Lı̀kɔ̀ndò li ŋkòyop minsòa; ŋ̀òò likɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀ jɛ̂m li ntoŋgı̀.

Lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀ li ŋkoblà.
Lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀ liy!
Lı̀kɔ̀ŋ jɔŋ li mpɛ̀k.
Lı̀kɔ̀ŋ li ɓe hola i jɔ̀ gwèt, jɔ̀ bı̀sàŋ, nolôl bı̀nùga tɔ̀ ɓôl ŋgambi.
Lı̀kɔ̀ŋ li kilɔ̂k li ŋkı̀ı̀ŋa hyààm.
Lı̀kɔ̀ŋ li mpihloŋgo.
Lı̀kɔ̀ŋ li ŋgaa li nluhūl mɛ̂!
Lı̀kɔŋga li kɔɔ li nlek i wɔ̌m.
Lı̀kɔ̀ɔ̀gàk nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋ̀kɔgɔɔ̄ nyɛ; lı̀kɔ̀ɔ̀gàk li nyoy.
Lı̀kɔ̀ɔ̀gɛnɛ li ntodoo li ŋkās.
Lı̀kɔ̀p njaŋgumba: ŋgèdà ù m̂mâl hɛ̂gɓa ɓɔ̂t njaŋgumba ndi tɔ̀ ù nlà kɔ̂p njaŋgumba kɛl ı̀pɛ. Ha nyɛ̄n ù gwèe kùndɛ̀ i kɛ̀ɛ̀p ı̀ yɔŋ ɓɔ̂t ù tablàk kı̀ ɓòt. I kɛ̄l mùt à nsūgus likɔ̀p njaŋgumba, à nnɔ̄l ŋgwɔ yɔ̀kɛl. Ɓa ɓe ɓenà kan yɔ ŋɛ̄mkède. Iɓālɛ̄ ù njɛ mû, wɛ̀ɛ ù ǹhemlɛ lɛ ù gakɔ̀p njaŋgumba, yàk wɛ̀ u nɔ̂l ı̀yɔ̀ŋ ɓòt ɓàpɛ ɓa jɛ, jɔn ŋgèn ı̀ni lɛ:.
Lı̀kɔy li hiɓoy.
Lı̀kɔ̀y ǹyòl; lı̀kɔ̀y hı̀ɓoy.
Lı̀kù li po.
Lı̀kube li kuyı̄ còòm.
Lı̀kube li mɓɛ̂blà.
Lı̀kube li nnyɔ̀da lɔŋgɛ̂ i nyɔ̀.
Lı̀kube lı̀tɔ̀mbga li ŋkɔ̀ŋla lɔŋgɛ̂.
Lı̀kuɓe li nnɛ̀ ŋgandàk.

Lı̀lembel li mudàa li ye kı̄isı̀n.
Lı̀lemês hɔp li ntɔ̄hlà.
Lı̀lemlɛ̀gɛ̀ li hikuu ŋgèdà nyɛ̀mb.
Lı̀lɛ̀bɛ li ɓê mbɔt ɓòdàà ɓa kwâŋ.
Lı̀lɛ̀dɛ̀k li hisi i ŋgèdà sèp.

Lı̀lɛgɛ̂k jee li pondı̂ li ntı̄s ɓe nɔp.
Lı̀lɛgɛ̂k jee li wɔɔ li ŋùnda lɛ à ńyàgàl.

Lı̀lɛlɛ̂k jɔŋ li nlɔŋ li mɓèbel mɛ̂!

Lı̀lɛlnà bı̀jɛk ǹlɔŋ li nlɔ lāa?
Lı̀lɛmɛ̂k i ŋgàndàk ǹsɔn.
Lı̀lɛ̀ndgà à bilɛ̀nda minhyōmok.
Lı̀lɛndlàk jee li ŋkono li ŋùnda lɛ à yè mùt wı̌m.

Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kɛ ı̄ lēp.
Màŋgɛ à ŋkɛ̄k komôl.
Màŋgɛ à ŋkɛ̄s likɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Màŋgɛ̀ à ŋ̀kidna i ɓèŋgɛ̀ mı̀ntùk.
Màŋgɛ à ŋkı̀s ɓɔɔ.
Màŋgɛ à ŋkı̀s kɛŋgɛɛ.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kôgaha mɛ ŋgwɔ̄.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kôm ni ŋŋɔ we.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kɔmɔ̄l kêgsɛ̀.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kûmla mɛ̂.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kwahal ɓɔ̂blà.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kwambāl manyâŋ.
Màŋgɛ à ŋkwɛ̄ɛ mis.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀kwɔ lı̄sè li njâl.
Màŋgɛ à ŋ̀ubi ŋgwee.
Màŋgɛ kı̄la à ŋkūdûp.
Màŋgɛ lı̀pàmàl nû!
Màŋgɛ màɓun.
Màŋgɛ mı̀ndaŋ à m̂ɓanda manyâŋ.
Màŋgɛ mudàa à m̂pak biɓumbuu gwee, nyɛ lı̀ɓiı̂ li mɓɛp nyɛ mbɔ̀m.
Màŋgɛ mudàa à ǹcik maŋgɛ mûnlom.
Màŋgɛ mudàa nu ɓɔ hilɔ̄ga hı̂, ɓa bigwālna man.
Màŋgɛ mudàa nunu à ńyı̄ mbaŋgō.
Màŋgɛ mudàa nunu à ńyı̄ mpàŋgo.
Màŋgɛ mûnlom à ncōk bitòŋ.
Màŋgɛ mûnlom nunu à nsāl ŋgandàk.
Màŋgɛ nu à gwèèɓa.
Màŋgɛ nû à ǹnyɛmɛl ŋgɔ̂k.
Màŋgɛ nu à ǹyɔlā hana.
Màŋgɛ nû à ŋ̀kahal kōgı̂.
Màŋgɛ nû à ŋkwēlɛ ɓe mɛ pāk.
Màŋgɛ nû à ŋkwɛ̄hɛl jogà.
Màŋgɛ nunu.
Màŋgɛ nunu à biābal pee ni mɔ̀ɔ.
Màŋgɛ nunu à biyɔ̄dlà, à kahal kwɛ̀l i tı̀ ɓôt.
Màŋgɛ nunu à gwèe lı̀saha.
Màŋgɛ nunu à gwèe lı̀seha.
Màŋgɛ nunu à gwèe yı̄.
Màŋgɛ nunu à mbı̄ɛ ɓe tɔ jàm.
Màŋgɛ nunu à mɓèna gwô.
Màŋgɛ nunu à mɓèna leŋel ɓes.
Màŋgɛ nunu à nhādɓɛnɛ bilı̀yà gwee; ù hadɓɛnɛ ɓâŋ mɛ̀.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ǹholol hana.
Màŋgɛ nunu à nhyɔ̄ŋɔp ŋgandàk.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋànnɛ i jòl li isāŋ nu à ŋ̀ûn.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋgwēs nyɛgı̄.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋ̀kaābɛ i ɓèdı̀ sɛ̀l i ŋgı̀i kɛ̄l.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋkēnd ɓe lɛ̂n!
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋ̀kɛŋɛ̂p!
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋ̀kɔlɔ̄l mɛ nı̀ wı̌p.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋkɔ̀n yiindà ye wɔ̀ŋi.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋ̀kwês jɛm hana.
Màŋgɛ nunu à ŋ̀lɛgɛp i ɛ̄mblɛ̀ ŋ̀kwɛ̀l.
Màŋgɛ nunu à yè dûm.
Màŋgɛ nunu à yè los.
Màŋgɛ nunu nyɛn à mɓàà mindaŋ hi ŋgèdà i tı̀ ɓɔngɛ.
Màŋgɛ nuu à m̂ɓɔyɔp hay à ŋ̀kwɔ kêgsɛ̀.
Màŋgɛ nuu à ǹhambap hay i pɛ̀s ɓàkèn ɓa nlama yên.
Màŋgɛ nuy à nhɛ̄hɛl hay i pāŋ jùu.
Màŋgɛ nyɛn à m̂ɓɛ̂mɓɛnɛ i wı̌ndà ndi à tı̂mbhɛ mɛ̂.
Màŋgɛ nyɛn à ǹhimblɛ mɛ ŋwɛ̀mɛl.
Màŋgɛ nyɛn à ŋ̀kidha mɛ i njɛ̀l.
Màŋgɛ ŋwı̀i jwɛ̀m.
Màŋgɛ sǔglù à biɓēma yani ŋgandàk.
Màŋgɛ sǔglù à ǹheha mɛ ɓàɓɔ̀blà; dı̀ ǹheha ndâmb liēn.
Màŋgɛ sǔglù à ŋkɔ̀n masù.
Màŋgɛ wānda à ŋ̀kɔ̂l bitòŋ à umbɛ̂.
Màŋgɛ wānda nunu à nnɔ̄ga ŋgandàk.
Màŋgɛ̀lɛ̀ à nnēŋes bilɔ̀lɔ̀.
Màŋgɛŋgɛ̂s ma ye ŋkɔ̀ŋ wɔŋ ŋgàndàk.
Mǎŋgòlò ma nhōolɛnɛ ndèè sèp.
Mǎŋgòlò ma nsêmha mɔmasô.
Mǎŋgòlò mɛ̂m mâ!
Màŋgudga ma tuyɛ ma ŋkònha wɔŋi inyùu bı̀kɛŋi gwap.
Màŋwɛ̀mɛl mâ.
Màŋwı̀ı̀ ma ɓatòlò ma nloŋâ.
Màǒmàò à ǹyilı̄s nyɛ mı̌s njɔ̂ynjɔ̀y.
Màòŋg ma ta ɓē nyɛ màlam.
Màɔ̀k ma bilèndha nyɛ lɛ à ɓɔ̀ŋ ɓe jâm.
Màɔ̀k ma lien.
Màɔ̀k ma lien ma nlɛgı̂.
Màɔ̀k ma lien ma nsùlhà, ɓa nsûlhà.
Màɔ̀k ma nnùmb munu kùmba ini; pɔɔ yɔ̂ŋ ı̀ nnùmb.
Màɔ̀k ma nnyobâ.
Màɔ̀k ma nnyuha nyɛ mbòŋ? dı̀ nnyūha maɔ̀k.
Màɔ̀k ma ntɛ̂ŋ.
Màɔ̀k ma ŋgaŋ nı̀ tòŋ ŋgaŋ, màhàk.
Màɔ̀k ma ŋgûy ma nti kôn u liɓàà.
Màɔŋ ma ndap.
Mǎp ma taɓē nyɛ.
Màpam i mbāy sǔglù.
Màpam ma sûglù.
Màpemel ma Yesù.
Màpɛp ma ɓendi.
Mapɛ̄p mana ma ŋādlana ndigi ı̄ ŋgèdà ma ye ı̄kède màlep.
Màpɛp mɔŋ ma mɓēnda ɓēe.
Màpubi ma kɛl; nı̀ ɓòt ɓa ye màpubi.
Màpubi ma lambɛ̀ ma mɓèyey mɛ̂.
Màpubi màkɛŋi ma nsè mis.
Màpùna ma ta ɓe jâm li mût bı̀nàm.
Màpùnà ma ta ɓēe jâm li mût bı̀nàm.
Mardokai à bikān mbɔt ye kı̀i à ŋ̀kôs ɓeba ŋgân.
Màsa mes ma nnumhà, mbɔt yes i nnumhà.
Masà wɛ̀m nû!
Màsak ma nlēmel wɛ̂.
Màsak ma ńyɔŋā nyɛ.
Màsày ma nnùmb ɓeba njı̂ŋ.
Màsèbi ma ntı̄bil liɓimbɛ̂.
Màsɛ̀ɛ ma lien ma ndēŋgel mbɛ̀bi.
Màsɛk ma njɛ ńyòl ndap wɔsô.
Màsɛŋ ma ŋɔ̀ i ɓūm yee.
Màsı̀ ma njâl ma mɓèna nɛnnɛ i ŋgèdà gwèt.
Màsı̂n ma ntı̀ŋha lɔ̂.
Màsı̂ŋ à ǹhɛndɛp i njɛ̌l mbāy yɔ̂ŋ; hɛndɛp hana mbus ndāp.
Màsı̂ŋ à ŋkɛ̀ makulı̂.
Màsı̂ŋ à ŋkɛ̀ makundı̂.
Màsı̂ŋ à ŋ̀ɔŋ; njɛɛ à ŋ̀ɔŋ hisèse?
Màsı̂ŋ à tee ŋ̀kɔŋ.
Màsı̂ŋ ma mbaŋgō.
Màsı̀ŋ ma nlèdes ɓɔŋgɛ.
Màsı̀ŋ ma yenɛ̀ nsɛ̄ŋ isi.
Màsı̀s mâ ma ŋkwēha lɔŋgɛ̂.
Màsı̀s mɛ̂m ma ńyɔɔ̀.
Màsòbhɛ̀ ù ɓeē i tı̀ yɔŋ.
Màsòhbɛ̀ ma mɓèe.
Màsok ma sûglù ma kolı̄ nı̀ kɔgsɛ̀.
Màsok mana!
Màsomboo ma ntòl i Ndòk Tindı̄ Màkay.
Màsòs ma hikòa.
Màsòs ma tuyɛ̂; màtèmb ma tuyɛ̂.
Màsɔ ma mût mɔ̀k ma nhōlos mâm màɓɛ.
Màsɔna mā mût mɔ̀k ma nhōlos mâm màɓɛ.
Màsùmblɛ̀ ma ɓakı̀l i ŋgèdà ɓa ŋkɛ ı̄ ūgɛ ŋgɔ̀nd yǎp.
Màsùynɛ ma mbêŋ.
Màta ma soŋ.
Màta ma soŋ ma nsùu lihɛp.
Màtam ma bɛɛ ma nseēs ŋkɔ̀kɔ̂n.
Màtam ma kâk ma ntı̄bla masulûk.
Màtam ma kɔmbɔɔ ma njēba mɓòmôk.
Màtam ma lihat li hisi hyes màhɔgi lɛ kàlàsı̂n nı̀ gôl.
Màtam ma nsɛ̂glà.
Màtam ma ŋkahal yɔ̄ı̂.
Màtam ma ŋkahal yɔ̄yı̂.
Màtanga ma ŋkwɔ̀.
Màtàt ma ntomba.
Màteâk ma mâm.
Màtèmb nı̀ mbus à heha nyàgà lı̀kus i mbūs.
Màten mɔ mmaà ma ŋom tûk gwêt.
Matɛ̀mbɛ̀ɛ̀ mana! I nnɛ̄nɛ lɛ njɔ̀k ı̀ ǹtagɓɛnɛ hana.
Màtiàs Mbɛ̀m à nsɛ̀ɛ̀ ɓôt nyɛ̌mb màcèl
Màtihlɛ ma Yesù.
Màtı̀bil ma ŋaŋ.
Màtı̀là mɔŋ ma ta ɓē malam.
Màtı̀là wɛ̀m à nhɔ̄ɔ nsɔn.
Màtı̀lâs ma nsùgut, ǹsùgut u hiòndɛ̀.
Màtı̀lâs mee ma ńyɔɔ̄ masày.
Màtoà à higi i kòò u mbus.
Màtoà à ǹsoobɛ i lı̀ɓɔ̀ɔ̀.
Màtoà à ǹsoobɛ i ndɔ̀bɔ̀.
Màtoà à nsùhna nyɛ i tisɔ̀n.
Màtoà à ǹtɛɛ̄ kɛmbɛ̂.
Màtoà à ŋ̀kwɔ̂, à mpèbà ɓe.
Màtoà ma ɓòmol ŋgwɔ̄ lɛ̀n manâ, hanânɔ ŋ̀gwɔ ı̀ ı̀ m̂ɓɔ̂l ha ı̄ mbàà ǹlɔŋ matoà.
Màtoà ma ŋkwɔ̂, ndi ɓòt ɓa mpam cɛt.
Màtoà mɔŋ ma nhoo mɛ ŋgàndàk.
Màtoà sonda ı̀ ɓa nɔ̂ŋ nı̀ tòhtòs ma ēda ɓēē.
Màtol ma ntòl i ŋkɔ̀ŋ wɔŋ.
Màtowà à m̂pâk ù jòp ha ɓâŋ mû!
Màtowà à ŋòm.
Màtowà ma ŋkwêl nyɛ nsɛ̀ndi.
Màtoy ma nɔp hı̀kaŋ ma ŋkwɔ̀ nsɛ̀nɛ̀ ǹsɛ̀nɛ̀.
Màtoy ma sɛmkendi mā ŋkwɔ̀ nsɛ̀nɛ̀ ǹsɛ̀nɛ̀.
Màtɔn màtɔn.
Màtɔ̀ɔ̀ndɛ̀ ma hiɓɛ̀ɛ.
Màtɔ̀p ma nhaŋha ni hı̀si.
Màtùgɛ̀ ma Yesù.
Màu nı̀ mǔs dı̀lɔ dinâ tɔ̀ hı̀lɔ mɛ̀ kɛ̂ ɓe.
Màu nı̀ mǔs dı̀lɔ ditân.
Màwanda ma mɓı̀gdànà.
Màwanda ma mpūgna mɔɔ.
Màwanda ma ntɛlɛp i tān ma kahal pèèyànà.
Màwanda ma ntı̀lna bikààt.
Màwanda ma ńyēgnà ɓe.
Màwanda ma ńyēŋnà.
Màwanda ma ŋɛ̄bna bikààt.
Màwanda map maa.
Màwanda mɛ̂m ma nhooŋga mɛ mūnu i ŋgànd mɛ̀ ɓak mɛ̀ gwèe.
Màwanda mɛ̂m ma ńyigis mɛ ɓòt i mbāy.
Màye ma kɛl sɔndɛ̂ nyɛn Ŋwɛ̀t Yesù à tùgɛ i sɔ̀ŋ.
Màyel ma kɛl.
Màyɛ ma kɛl.
Màyɛ ma sêp; màyɛ sèp.
Màyi ma mâm.
Màyo ma pɔɔ.
Màyɔ ma nlòl limùt lii haa.
Màyɔ̀ɔ̀ ma njeē.
Màyɔ̀ɔ̀ ma ntomba.
Màyɔ̀ɔ̀ ma ńyòl.
Màyɔ̀ɔ̀ mɔŋ ma nyòl ma ye ɓɛ̀bɛ̀ɛ̀ nı̀ jàà li ndap.
Màyɔt ma gweē mɛ̀.
Mbàà tuyɛ ı̀ yè lɔŋgɛ ı̄ lihyumul.
M̀bàbàgà à heeba dı̀lɛ̀ŋgwɔ.
Mbàbi ɛ yɔŋ ı̀ mpōha ɓē.
Mbàbi i bɛɛ i ŋ́wêblà.
Mbàbi sı̀bŋgàŋ.
Mbàblà nyùu ı̀ gwèe mɛ̀.
Mbada lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mbàdgà ı̀ mɓèda hana lɛ̀n, dı̀ ǹlama tı̂mbhɛ yɔ̂.
Mbàdgà yɔ̌ŋ ı̀ gwèe mànɔ̀ɔ̀dànà.
Mbàeŋ ı̀ nyàgà ı̀ tà ɓe nugā ɓa jɛ.
Mbagdà ɓakihɔ̄p ɓa ditɛ̀ɛ̀ndɛ̀ diɓaà.
Mbagdà ditɛ̀ɛ̀ndɛ̀ diaâ.
Mbagdà ditɛ̀ɛ̀ndɛ̀ diɓaà.
Mbàghɛ̀ à ŋkɔ̀n ɓe nyɔɔ yɔ̀ kı̀kı̀i yɔ̀ wɔ̀ŋi.
Mbàgi sēp; pemês mbàgi.
Mbagla màten.
Mbahâl cèe.
Mbahâl inyùu bı̀hɛ̀là.
Mbàhàl ı̀ gwèe mɛ̀.
Mbahâl ı̀ ŋ̀kùs wɛ̂m.
Mbàhgɛ̀ i nnɔl sɔsɔ̄ pēe.
Mbàk ı̀ yè ɓeba kɔ̂n ikède lɔ̀ŋ; nunu mùt à ŋkɔ̀n mbâk.
Mbalɛ̀ ı̀ sòli.
Mbǎm ùm i kond wɛ̂ ù sɛ̂hlà wɛ̀ɛ ù gwèe lı̀ɓua.
Mbàmbà i mpàn i mɓèna ɓana mbôŋ.
Mbàmbà m̂pàn.
Mbàmbàgà mùdàa.
Mbàmbàŋgà mùdàa.
Mbàmbàt ı̀ mɓām.
Mbàmbàt ı̀ ǹsês mɛ̂!
Mbamgà mùt.
Mbàn lɔp, mbàn amb.
Mbàndà yèe ı̀ ǹloòhà.
Mbaŋg cèe ı̀ ǹsundı̀.
Mbaŋg cèe; mbaŋg bı̀hès.
Mbara lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mbàs ı̀ ǹhambâ.
Mbàs ı̀ni ı̀ yè holo; holo ŋɔ.
Mbay mbɔmbɔ̀k ı̀ yè lı̀ɓok.
Mbay nyɛ̀ga ı̀ ŋgwèlha hisɔ̂n.
Mbay yâp ı̀ m̂ɓɛp yaga liɓɛbɛ̂k jɔlisô.
Mbay yâp ı̀ yè mbay lı̀hat.
Mbay yeē ı̀ ǹtola lipènd.
Mbay yɛ̂m ı̀ yè ŋwɛ̀ɛ.
Mbay yɛ̂m ı̀ni.
M̀bayɛ̀ yɔn i ntı̄ miŋkòo ɓa ŋkèŋel miŋgɔndɔ.
Mbedel màɔ̀k.
Mbedge yɛ̂m ı̀ m̂pût, yɔ̀ŋ kı̂ ı̀ gapǔt.
Mbegde ŋ̀kɔ̀ŋ.
Mbèhèl ı̀ tà ɓe.
Mbèlà ı̀ yè ɓɛ̀bɛ̀ɛ̀.
Mben ı̀ ŋkàl lɛ ù ǹnɔl ɓâŋ.
Mbên u ŋgaŋgò u mɓugı̂.
Mbèna jɛ̄.
Mbend ı̀ ǹsiā nyɛ.
Mbèndɛ̀ jàm.
Mbènɛ̀ mbɔk!
Mbèŋ ı̀ ǹsuyı̀.
Mbeŋg lı̀ɓàdò.
Mbɛ̀bi ı̀ nhòŋ ɓiı̀m.
Mbɛ̀bi ı̀ nhùŋul ŋ̀ɔ mbɔk.
Mbɛ̀bi ı̀ nnùdul biɛ isı̄; mbɛ̀bi ı̀ nhòŋ.
Mbɛbi ı̀ ǹseēɓaha likɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mbɛ̀bi ı̀ ǹsêk, mbɛ̀bi ı̀ ǹsɛm.
Mbɛ̀bi ı̀ ǹtoyha malep i bɛ̀ɛ; màlep nı̀ màcèl ma ntōyhà.
Mbɛ̀bi tɔ̀ hyàŋgaa bi nnūmus mbɔt.
Mbɛ̀dɛ̀ màŋgà.
Mbɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀ ı̀ mɓāy mɛ ı̄ ŋŋɔ̄.
Mbɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀ ı̀ mɓāya i ŋŋɔ̄.
Mbɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀ ı̀ ńyèt sı̂ŋsı̀ŋ.

Mbɛy mùt.
Mbida bitɔ̀gɔ̀ɔ̀.
Mbiŋg ı̀ ŋkwɔ̀ ɓe nsɔ.
Mbı̀gdà nyɛ̌mb mùt.

Mbı̀nd ı̀ m̂ɓoo nyɛ.

Mbı̀ŋ jàm.
Mbı̀ŋ lı̀kas li ndap.
Mbòda bı̀jɛk; mbòda ɓɔ̌n.

Mbògi ŋ̀kaa.
Mbògi ŋ̀kaa ı̀ ǹnyêndlaha mɛ mɔ̀ɔ; dı̀ ǹnyêndlaha mɔɔ.
Mbogôl yàda, mbogôl jwɛ̀m.
Mbǒl yɔn ɓa mɓòŋol ɓakàlɛ̀.
Mbòlò ı̀ ŋ̀gwià mɛ lɛ̀n i ŋkùmɛ̀.
Mbom mùt ı̀ ǹsɔbɔ̄p i yèènɛ.
Mbom mùt ı̀ni ı̀ m̂ɓɛhna mɛ mǎn isı̄ ŋgèdà à kwɔ̌k.
Mbom mùt ı̀ni ı̀ ǹsiŋı̄p ni ikède ndāp sǔglù.
Mbòmà à ŋkɔ̀ŋa ɓe ŋgôŋ i jɛ̄.
Mbombo à binēŋha ɓes inyùulɛ̄ dı̀ bijɛ̄ ŋgandàk bı̀tòdò.
Mbombo à m̂pând ndap ni kidı̂k i ɓɛndɛ.
M̀bombo à ǹcebes ŋgandàk cèe.
Mbombo à ǹlamb sûp cɔ̀bi.
Mbombo à ǹtulus ŋgandàk màŋ.
Mbombo à ŋ̀gwol mɛ jɔ̌mb li cɔbı̄.
Mbòmbòt ı̀ mǎn ı̀ yè màtadgà.
Mbòmdà ı̀ ǹheya nyɛ yàlâk.
M̀bon i nnɛ̄ɛbɛ ûm ŋgèdà ŋgɔ̀nd ûm i ntōp nyɛ.
Mbon lı̀kwɛ̀ɛ̀, mbon mbɔmbɔ̀k, mbon ŋgê, mbon m̂maŋ ntoŋ.
Mbòndo ı̀ m̂mâl i ŋɛ̄gɛl mɛ màsɔ̌ŋ.
Mbòndo ı̀ ntı̄ moo màlam.
Mbònjı̀ i nnùmb lɔŋgɛ njı̂ŋ.

Mbònjı̀ ı̀hɔgi i nnùmb laɓı̄ndà.
M̀boŋ yɔŋ ŋ̀kaa ı̀ nlɔ̂ ɛ̀?

Mɛ̀ mɓāghɛnɛ kwadɛ i kùmba yɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ mɓāghɛnɛ nyɛ kwādɛ.

Mɛ̀ mɓāhla ni ǹsɔn matı̀là.

Mɛ̀ mɓāhlɛ wɛ cèe.

Mɛ̀ mɓàmb cɔbı̄.

Mɛ̀ m̂ɓâŋ siŋil i ɓɛndɛ.

Mɛ̀ ǹlama ɓâdɓà tɔ̀ɔ mɛ̀ ŋgwēs ntɔhɔ̂l wɛ̀m.
Mɛ̀ ǹlama pam i ɓěnı̄ lɛ̂n.
Mɛ̀ ǹlama sombol ɓɔn ɓɛ̂m bı̂k hi ŋwii sǔglù ı̀ mɓòdòl.
Mɛ̀ ǹlama ti bikwàk inyùu yɔ̌m mɛ̀ binı̄mis wɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹlandɛ nyɛ.
Mɛ̀ ǹlebā mɔnı̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹlebel wɛ bı̀nan.
Mɛ̀ ǹlelel lep i mòŋgo.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̄ɛgɛ ɓe mɛ hɔ̄p wee.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̄ɛŋgɛ ni mbēgde.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̄l nɛ̂n i mùnɛ: mɛ̀ ŋ̀ek wɔm tɔ̀ lı̀kòlòl u ŋkolà ɓee
Mɛ̀ ǹlɛla ŋkɔ̀k.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɛ̂ŋ à om kaŋŋ!
Mɛ̀ ǹlɛ̂ŋ koy hı̀kɔ̀ŋgɔ̀ hi ŋgaa hyada.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̀ŋ ndêk biɓūk hana i ɓɔ̀ma wanda.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̄ŋ nyɔɔ̄ ŋgàndàk.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɛ̂ŋ ŋgɔ̂k malēp ı̀ kwɔ lɛ cùŋgum.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɛ̂ŋ ŋgɔ̂k munu malēp dı̀ŋgii di pam.
Mɛ̀ nlɛ̄ŋɛl i ɓòm.
Mɛ̀ ǹligis wɔm wɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ nlò matuba ma ńyòl; lò hı̀ɓɛ̀ɛ.
Mɛ̀ ǹlobol nyûŋ còbi; mɛ̀ ǹlobol i hyɔ̀bi hini i kàya.
Mɛ̀ ǹlohbɛ undā manjɛ̀l i tı̀là ɓàsàa.
Mɛ̀ ǹlohlɛnɛ pân nı̀ ŋgɔ̀k.
Mɛ̀ ǹlôl i Dı̀yɛ̂; mɛ̀ ǹlôl i màtoà; mɛ̀ ǹlôl ɓe mɛ wɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹlôl wɛ ŋ̀kèn.
Mɛ̀ ǹlomsɛ hɔp wɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹlondlɛ ŋwɛt ŋgûy mɔmasô à ǹtı̂mbhɛ mɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹloŋōl mambɔt i ɓɔ̀t.
Mɛ̀ ǹloŋōl mel mu hı̄ndāma.
Mɛ̀ ǹloŋol ŋgɔmbı̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹloōhɛnɛ ŋgând Paskà yak ɓɔ̀n ɓɛ̂m
Mɛ̀ ǹloōs kêgsɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹloōs makègsɛ̀; à ǹloōs nyɛ kɔ̀n.
Mɛ̀ nlɔ̀ ɓe mɛ ı̂l wɛ̀ wɔ̌m.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔ̂ i kòla i wɛ̀ɛnı̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔ ı̄ ɓěnı̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔ ı̄ wɛ̌nı̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔ lɛ̂n kobā! kòba ŋgèdà; kòba ni eaaǹg.
Mɛ̀ nlɔ̀ nɔmâ; mɛ̀ bilɔ̀ nɔmâ.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔŋɔl ŋwii u tolò.
Mɛ̀ nlɔ̀ɔ̀ wɛ ŋwı̀i.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔp limbòò.
Mɛ̀ ǹlɔp ŋgàndàk cɔ̀bi.
Mɛ̀ nlūga kwadɛ nı̀ m̂pòs.
Mɛ̀ nnāhla njâl.
Mɛ̀ ǹnâŋlɛ i kède màtoa.
Mɛ̀ ǹnedel liwanda jɛ̂m hı̀òndɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹnedēs ɓɔŋgɛ màkègsɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɛɛbɛ jàm ù ŋkàl.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɛɛbɛ wɛ lɛ̀n.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɛɛɓɛnɛ jàm lini mahɛ̂l.
Mɛ̀ nnɛ̀ɛ̀mbɛ pubus mbay.
Mɛ̀ nnɛ̄k ɓe nyɛ.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɛ̂t nyɛ ŋgèlè ɓâ; hı̀ŋgɔ̀ndà hyɔŋ hi nnɛt kêgsɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹnidı̄s nyɛ ɓūm yɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹnimis bikààt gwɛ̂m bi sǔglù.
Mɛ̀ ǹniŋı̄ man.
Mɛ̀ nnı̄iga ɓɔŋgɛ lı̀ɔŋ bı̀sɛ̀l.
Mɛ̀ nnı̀ŋ.
Mɛ̀ ǹnı̀ŋnɛ ı̄ sı̀mɛ̂t.
Mɛ̀ ǹnı̂ŋnɛ man i kàgà.
Mɛ̀ ǹnogol wɛ jàm.
Mɛ̀ nnōk njoghɛ̀ i ŋɛ̄m, ŋɛm u ŋkwɔ̀ mɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹnomōl i nyɔ̄ màɔ̀k.
Mɛ̀ nnòŋha mût wı̌p sondâ; sondâ i nnòŋha mût wı̌p.
Mɛ̀ nnòŋol nyɛ njàŋ i maɓàl.
Mɛ̀ nnòŋos tolo siŋgı̂.
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̄gɓɛnɛ i lēp.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔgɔp malēp mâ, cǒs di ta mɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̄k hɔ̂gɓɛ̀ nyɔ̀nɔ, mɛ̀ gwèe hɔ̀gɓɛ̀ nyɔ̀nɔ.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk kiŋ ı̀ nsèbèl.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk kiŋ yeē màlı̀i màlı̀ı̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk kugukùgù ndòmlɛ mùt à njɔ̀ ɓɔ ŋwàa i tùŋ.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk lɛ ù ǹlek, ası̀ya àŋ!
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̄k manyı̀i i ŋgèda wɛ̀ ù njɛ̄ nyaā bitòŋ.
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̄k ması̀hı̀ i ŋgèdà mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ mût à ŋ̀kɛ̂gɓà.
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̄k mɓegla.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk ndigi kūglukùglù, ndòmlɛ bı̀sàŋ bı̂!
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔk ŋkùmbgà u nɔp.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔl ɓasɔ̀wa ɓācògɛ mɛ̀ amb yàni.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔl hilo ni ndàmb.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔl hitòn i wɔ̀m wɛ̂m nı̀ ŋgaa.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔl nyɔɔ, ndi ı̀ ŋgi kɔɔŋà ha ı̄ mbēdge.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔl sɔa nı̀ ndàmb.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔŋɔ̄k nyɛ, à hyɔl.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔŋɔ̄k nyɛ mɛ̀ at.
Mɛ̀ ǹnɔŋɔ̄k nyɛ, mɛ̀ kobol nyɛ i tı̀ maɔ̀k.
Mɛ̀ nnɔ̀ɔ̀dɛ nyɛ nı̀ màmbàdgà;
Mɛ̀ nnùŋlɛnɛ nyɛ mòo.
Mɛ̀ ǹnuŋūl kop dı̀koo diaâ.
Mɛ̀ ǹnûp hitɛ̀bɛ̀ i lɔ̄p.
Mɛ̀ nnùp hyimba hı̄ kop; cı̀mba dı̄ ŋgôs nı̀ di kundi...ikb. di ɓê bı̀ɛ̀ŋg bi gwêt bi man ɓàsàa.
Mɛ̀ ǹnuūɓɛnɛ mandap ma mawanda mɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹnuyɛ bijɛk.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyegi i kɛ̀ likè.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyiimbɛnɛ mût nyùŋga mòo.
Mɛ̀ nnyɔ̄ malep, mòo ma nnyɔ i mı̀ntumba.
Mɛ̀ nnyɔ̀ndɓɛ i lūk.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyɔndɔ̂p i lūk.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyɔɔ̄ŋga i kòò.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyuk li jàm.
Mɛ̀ ǹnyuūnɛ maɔ̀k inyùu njàl.
Mɛ̀ nogha ŋudu i jàm màlêt à ǹniiga i sǔglù; dı̀ ǹnogha i jàm lı̂.
Mɛ̀ nsāa tâs.
Mɛ̀ ǹsaɛnɛ nyɛ ndı̀ò.
Mɛ̀ ǹsagi nı̄!
Mɛ̀ nsāgna m̂ɓɔm.
Mɛ̀ ǹsahal ńyòl.
Mɛ̀ nsāk masaò.
Mɛ̀ nsāl.
Mɛ̀ ǹsal ŋgandàk, mɛ̀ nsòmbol hep ndêk.
Mɛ̀ nsàyap wɛ ŋwı̀ı̀ yɔndɔ ǹlam.
Mɛ̀ ǹsêbla mu ı̄ dı̄na lı̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹsêgha nyɛ bı̀tamb, dı̀ ǹsêgha bitamb gwes.
Mɛ̀ nsèghɛ baskò.
Mɛ̀ ǹsehēs ndap yɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹselel nyɛ njɔ̀ɔ.
Mɛ̀ nsēles ɓolō i mbāy.
Mɛ̀ ǹsembel nyɛ i wɔ̀m bɔ̂l.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛɛ ŋ̀kɔ̀k.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛgɛ̄l matam ma komôl.
Mɛ̀ nsɛ̀ghɛ fufu
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛ̂ghɛnɛ wɛ lı̀sɛgɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛ̂m ŋgandàk mɔ̀ni.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛndı̀; njɛ̌l ı̀ nsɛ̀ndı̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɛ̂ndnɛ i ŋgı̀i hı̀kòa.
Mɛ̀ nsiı̄ba nyɔɔ.
Mɛ̀ nsı̀hil ɓapàgi ni lı̀ŋgɛŋɛɛ.
Mɛ̀ ǹsı̂m ni!
Mɛ̀ nsı̄nd ni ŋgàndàk màkɔ̀n.
Mɛ̀ nsı̄ŋha nyuu.
Mɛ̀ nsı̄ŋil wɛ ndāp.
Mɛ̀ nsı̄ya mbɔt.
Mɛ̀ ǹsôblànà; ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa nsòblana moo.
Mɛ̀ ǹsogos likòga.
Mɛ̀ ǹsok hana.
Mɛ̀ nsòk pos i bɛɛ i kède ɓɛ̄ɛ.
Mɛ̀ nsòl mbɔt yɛ̂m i lēp.
Mɛ̀ nsòm têk.
Mɛ̀ ǹsoma wɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ nsòmblɛnɛ ɓee inyùu ɓòlo.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbol ɓa nhemlɛ̀ Nyambɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbol ɓe lindɛndɛ.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbol ɓe mɛ kàgdakàgdà wɔ̀ŋ!
Mɛ̀ nsòmbol ɓeebaha pɔ̂m yɛ̂m ǹtomba.
Mɛ̀ ǹsombol ɓɔŋgɛ bı̀hebtè.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbol ɓɔ̂t kɛmbɛ̂ i mbāy yɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹsombol man wɛ̀m bı̀kààt bi sûglù.
Mɛ̀ ǹsombol nyɛ kùmul liɓàdò.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbòl, wɛ̀ ti mɛ̀ ŋgaa.
Mɛ̀ nsòmbòl, wɛ̀ ti mɛ̀ ŋ̀gwɔ.
Mɛ̀ nsòŋa liɓɛ hana.
Mɛ̀ nsōoha man.
Mɛ̀ nsɔ̀bna i lūk.
Mɛ̀ nsɔ̄l gwoo i gwēl i majò.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb biɓɔ̀gɔ̀l bi nyagà.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb biednɛ bitân inyùu bı̀kààt mɛ̀ ŋɔ̄m i Kàmɛ̀rûn.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb bilolo i ɓòm.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb bitamb.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb galɔ̂ŋ mòò.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb makàlà nı̀ kùrùkurù.
Mɛ̀ ǹsɔmb yaŋyàŋ.
Mɛ̀ nsɔ̄mna wɛ̂ i lɔ̀ŋ, ɓa nsɔmna ɓɔɓâ yak ŋgɔ̄mı̂n.
Mɛ̀ nsɔ̄ŋgɔl mɔnı̄.
Mɛ̀ nsɔ̄ɔhɛ lɛ u ɓembnɛ mɛ̀ ɓana ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ.
Mɛ̀ nsùghɛ nyɔ̂, ɓa nsùghɛ malep i pōs.
Mɛ̀ ǹsuhūl i lı̀kàlà.
Mɛ̀ ntām makè ma mbay.
Mɛ̀ ntāt ɓɔŋgɛ.
Mɛ̀ ǹtebel wɛ̂ màɓàdò.
Mɛ̀ ntēdes ŋkɔ̀kɔ̂n.
Mɛ̀ ǹtee hiɓɛ̀ɛ̀ hi ı̄ jùu.
Mɛ̀ ntēedana bijɛk i ndùgi, nunu mùt à ntēedana ŋgandàk, ɓana ɓɔŋgɛ ɓa ntēedana ɓɔ nı̀ ɓɔ.
Mɛ̀ ǹtegi pân i ŋgı̀i jùdgà.
Mɛ̀ ǹtem luk.
Mɛ̀ ntèŋ ɓaka inyùu yàp i ŋwı̀ı̀ lep.
Mɛ̀ ntɛ̄hɛ didùn di ɓôt i ɓòm.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ gwɔm gwɔbisô, yɔ̌m i nheŋel mɛ̂ m̂ɓɔ̀m sibà.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ liɓɔ̀mɔ̀k jap.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ wɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ wɛ ù nhēŋ masɔ̀ŋ.
Mɛ̀ ntɛ̄p mambɔt i sābɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹti wɛ bāskò yàŋgà, ù helel ɓâŋ i gwàŋgà bi mâm.
Mɛ̀ ǹtibil linuhlɛ jɔŋ.
Mɛ̀ ǹtibil tostòs wɛ̀m.
Mɛ̀ ǹtiblaha tostòs wɛ̀m, ɓa ntiblaha ɓâp.
Mɛ̀ ǹtihɓa nyɔɔ.
Mɛ̀ ǹtimbı̄s mambɛ̀gɛ̀ɛ̀ inyùulɛ̄̄ kak i mpâk.
Mɛ̀ ntı̄ malêt wɛ̀m bı̀ɓegês inyùu ǹsɔn à bigwèlel mɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ntı̄ Nyambɛ màyègà inyùu màm màlam à mɓòŋol mɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ntı̄ wɛ bı̀jɛk.
Mɛ̀ ntı̄ wɛ bı̀yihnɛ lɛ ŋgɔ̀nd yɔ̌ŋ ı̀ ŋ̀gwâl.
Mɛ̀ ntı̄bil mɛ yı̄ kɔlɔŋ.
Mɛ̀ ntı̀ı̀mba top nlèlèm u hyembi.
Mɛ̀ ntı̀mbis ɓɔŋgɛ i ndāp inyùulɛ̄̄ nɔ̌p à nsòmbol nɔ.
Mɛ̀ ntı̀mhɛnɛ wɛ gwɔ̀m gwɔŋ bisū bi mboŋ ɓôt.
Mɛ̀ ntı̀p hɔp, tâ à ǹtı̂p ŋ̀kòò kɛmbɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ntōl mâŋ.
Mɛ̀ ǹtolnɛ malep i lēm mbuluk.
Mɛ̀ ǹtolol ı̂ni wɔm.
Mɛ̀ ǹtomōl biɓɛndɛ lı̀pam hı̄ɓūt.
Mɛ̀ ntòmol tɔnɛ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹtoŋha ŋgwɔ nùga; ŋgwɔ yes i ntoŋha nugā.
Mɛ̀ ntōŋos kaàt yɛ̀m lı̀gweê.
Mɛ̀ ntòòma maɓam.
Mɛ̀ ǹtoōs kɔɔ.
Mɛ̀ ntōos ŋgwɔ yɛ̂m nùga.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̄dɔl ɓe tɔ mùt.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɔhı̂.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɔhlà; jàm lı̂ li ntɔ̄hlà.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɔhlɛnɛ wɛ nyɛ̄.
Mɛ̀ ǹtɔl bitòdò.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̄ŋ maɓàdò mɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̀ɔ̀ matam ma kakāò.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̄ɔgɛ ɓalàl ɓɔŋ lɛ ɓa kı̂l mɛ̀ i lēp.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̀s gwiihà.
Mɛ̀ ntɔ̀yɛ ntɔ̌ygɛ̀ lɛ ŋ̀gwàŋ kɛl unu lɛ̀n.
Mɛ̀ ǹtubsa wɛ̂, njɛɛ à nlɔ̀ ?
Mɛ̀ nu mɛ̀ ŋkàŋda hana.
Mɛ̀ nunu ɓa mɓoyɛ nyɔnɔ̄ bikāy.
Mɛ̀ nunu mɛ̀ ɓâk mɛ̀ ŋkāgla njâl hana lɛ̀n.
Mɛ̀ nunu mɛ̀ ǹhendel i mùù lɔ̂m.
Mɛ̀ nunu mɛ̀ ŋ́wāŋla ni ǹsɔn hana i mbēdge.
Mɛ̀ ǹyegēs wɔm wɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹyek ɓɔ ɓa nlɛ̀ŋna biya.
Mɛ̀ ǹyek likwàkwaā munu i mbōm wɔ̀m wɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹyek ŋkɔ̀kɔ̂n à ŋgi hehlàk.
Mɛ̀ ǹyên i nɔ̀y i mbɛ̀ŋgɛ̀ caŋcaŋ soŋ i aaà.
Mɛ̀ ǹyeŋ bitamb gwɔŋ tɔ̀ ǹtɛhgɛ̀; ù gayēŋ mɛ nı̀ ŋwày.
Mɛ̀ ńyēŋ hiòndɛ̀ i tɔ̀tɔ̂p yɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ńyēŋ hɔma lɛ mɛ ɓɔŋɔp.
Mɛ̀ ǹyeŋɓa lɛ̂n i ɓɔ̀ma.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɛgɛ̄l sa wɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɛhɛ̄l nsɔn wɛ̂m lipàn.
Mɛ̀ nyɛn mɛ̀ m̂ɓehēl nugā i hyàndi, mɛ̀ gwèe ɓèhèl!
Mɛ̀ ńyɛ̄p ni mɔ̀ni ndi hà nı̀ bı̀ɓàŋga ɓe.
Mɛ̀ ǹyibı̄ kwɛm moo nı̀ m̂ɓɔ̀ɔ̀ lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹyilā mbɔlɔ̀ inyùu ɓàkɔ̀lɓà ɓɛ̂m.
Mɛ̀ ǹyimbɛ̄ wɛ̂, yàk mbɔt yɔŋ.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̄ ɓe i yɔ̌m mɛ̀ ncèèlɛnɛ nyɛ.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̄ ɓe jol jee.
Mɛ̀ nyı̄ ɓe tɔ̀ɔ à ŋ̀kɛ̂.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̄ i màm mana.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̄ luk baskò.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̀mbnɛ nyɛ lisāha je.
Mɛ̀ ǹyı̂p kwɛm nı̀ m̂ɓɔ̀ɔ̀ lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mɛ̀ ńyı̄s wɛ lɛ̄ ŋgɔ̀nd yɔ̌ŋ ı̀ ŋ̀gwâl.
Mɛ̀ ńyōnos pos nı̀ màlep.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɔba kı̀i mɛ̀ pɔdɔk, jɔn ɓòt ɓa nɔ̀lɔk makɛŋi.
Mɛ̀ ńyɔ̄ga inyùu tɔ̀ jàm; dı̀ yɔga ɓâŋ inyùu tɔ̀ jàm.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɔ̂n; ŋ̀kuu u ńyɔ̂n.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɔ̂ŋ kinı̂ munu kı̀i lı̀hɛp li nay.
Mɛ̀ ńyɔ̀ŋ makalâk lòŋnı̀ kɔglɔ likɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɔ̂ŋ yɛ̂m pɛ̀s i ŋkɔ̀ŋ.
Mɛ̀ ǹyɔp.

M̀maŋ mudàa unu u ŋāglà.
M̀maŋ mût u ńyı̀ŋyɛ̀.
Mogoo mût; megee mût.
Mòlol ma ntɔ̄y liɓàdò.
Mǒm ma ye ŋkɔ̀ŋ wɔŋ ŋgandàk.
Mòŋgo u bilèŋa i lɔ̀m.
Mòŋgo u leŋi ŋgı̀i màlep.
Mòŋgo u ncagna ɓes liyàgi hɛ̀ liɓōŋ ɓe.
Mòŋgo u nhōla i yàp lɔ̀m.
Mòŋgo u ntɛgɛp i màlep.
Mòŋgo u ŋkop.
Mòŋgo u ŋkop ɓòt ɓa pɛy nyɛ̂mb.
Mòo ma mɓɔ̀ŋ tɛ̂mtɛ̀m i pondı̄.
Mòò ma nhɔ̀y i kède màlep.
Mòò ma njâp ma nnɛ̀ ni ǹlamb.
Mòò ma ntɔ̀gà.
Mòò mɔŋ ma ye lı̀layɛ̂.
Môsè à ɓa gwelèl ǹtɔŋgɔ i pamnà lòk yudà isı̄ likàk.
Mòy ma bilàŋ ma nlɛ̀t i yı̄.
Mɔm ŋwɛ̀ɛ.
Mɔm u ŋgôy u yê m̂ɓoŋgo ; ŋgàbà lı̀en ı̀ ı̀ ŋ̀koōbana i pemês màɔ̀k.
Mɔndɔl ŋ̀kɔ̀kɔ̂n nu à yè wɛ̀ ha ı̄ pāŋ.
Mɔ̀ni à ǹhup i jɔ̌mb.
Mɔ̀ni à ǹyilā hibı̄ hyɔbı̄ munu lɔ̀ŋ yes.
Mɔ̀ni à ǹyilā nyɛ ŋgı̀m nyambɛ̂!
Mɔ̀ni à yè kɛ̀y à yè kı̀ pebà.
Mɔ̀ni ɓa nnip à sòlnɛ i bı̀kay.
Mɔ̀ni mi nsɔt, nyùŋga ı̀ ǹsɔt.
Mɔ̀ni mi ńyı̄ŋâ.

Mɔ̀ni wɔ̂ŋ vanɛ à yè hɛɛ?

Mùdàa à kɔba ŋ̀kono i ɓòm Liyòŋ, à ɓɔ̀ɔ̀wàk wɔ, à ablàgà ndi à ɓɔ̀ɔ̀wàk à ablàgà, ɓɔ nyɛ lɛ weeêy! ki yɔ ŋkōno û u ɓāk wɛ nı̀ jàm ɛ̀?

Ndondoo ı̀ ǹyeglɛ nyɛ likègee.
Ndòŋ hyanda ı̀ni ı̀ ntòl ɓe.
Ndoŋ lɔ̀lɔ̀k; lɔ̀lɔ̀k mût.
Ndoŋgi yɛ̂m ı̀ni.
Ndòy i hɔgi i mɓāy.
Ndòy ı̀ nsànd kop.
Ndòy ı̀ ǹtobna man kōp; dı̀nùni di ntōbna mis.
Ndòy ı̀ ŋ̀gwɛ̂l mɛ kōp.
Ndòy ı̀ ŋ̀kɛ ı̀ ɓɛdɛp ŋgı̀i ɛ̄ haà.
Ndòy ı̀ ŋkùyɓaha nyɔɔ̀.
Ndɔga wɛ̂m u nnɛ̄.
Ndɔk ı̀ wɔ̂k ɓâŋ ı̀ tɛhgɛ̀ ndigı̂.
Ndɔk yeē yɔ̌n ı̀ biyùyha mɛ i màn nunu.
Ndɔk yɔ̂ŋ ı̀ ńyàmb ɓalêt.
Ndɔmbɔɔ ı̀ nhōla ɔŋ biɓuŋgâ.
Ndɔn i ńyèènɛ i hōk.
Ndɔ̀ndɛ̀ njèe ı̀ ǹjɛ kɛmbɛ̂.
Ndɔ̀ndɛ̀ nùga.
Ndɔ̀ndɔ̀k ǹluŋ ı̀ yè tiblɛ mapɔɔ.
Ndɔ̀ndɔ̀k yɔ̌n ı̀ bilēmes nyɛ.
Ndɔ̀ŋ ı̀ yè yɔ̀m i mintùk inyùu ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ.
Ndùdù yɛ̀m ı̀ kòli ɓēe ni mùt m̂pɛ.
Ndùgdà ı̀ ɓak ma gwɛ̀l man.
Ndùgi ı̀ yè teedana bijɛk.
Ndùhi ı̀ nlòs makɛŋi; ɓòt ɓa kwâŋ ɓa ɓe lɛ̂ŋ ŋgaa ni ndùhi.
Ndùtù yɛ̀m ı̀ kòli ɓē ni mùt m̂pɛ.
Neegà jâm.
Nèèmbaha lɛ̄ mɛ̀ ǹlamb wɔŋ; dı̀ ǹneēmbaha diɓɛ̀ɛ di bijɛk.
Neiha ŋɛm.
Nèndes nyɛ̄ màlep ma nyɔ.
Neŋha mût i heeba ŋ̀kanda.

Neyha ŋɛm.
Nɛ̀ɛ̀mbɛnɛ mɛ̀ unu ǹlamb.
Ǹhatōm à m̂pôdna miŋkɛk mi tom nı̀ ǹlohâ.
Ǹheblàk koy u ŋôhɓɛnɛ i hyɛ̀ŋ.

Ǹhêmlɛ̀ màmben ma lɔ̂ŋ à ŋkòs ɓee ndudù.

Nigı̂l ŋgı̀m ɓòlo.
Niglaha mɛ̀ mǎn nunu màtı̀là ma yɔndɔ; ɓa nniglaha matı̀là ma yɔndɔ.
Niglak, ŋwǎs bı̄lɛ̄ŋɛ̂l bı̂ ù mɓɔ̀ŋ hanânɔ.
Niigaha màn wɔ̂ŋ; ɓàlêt ɓa nniigàhà.
Niigana mɛ̀ nyɛ i jàm lini; ɓa nnı̄igana biɓeba bi mâm.
Nı̀ hı̀si hi ha bijɛk hookō.
Nı̀ hyomna ɓâŋ yɔ̀m bikwà binân.

Ǹsà gwɔ̌m à ǹlɔ̂!

Nyambɛ à yè ǹsaŋ Ŋwɛ̌t wês Yesù Krı̌stò.
Nyambɛ nyɛ̄n à ńyı̄ ɓaɓòŋòl ɓee.
Nyambɛ nyɛn à ńyı̄ ɓagwèlèl ɓee.
Nyambɛ nyɛ̄n à ŋŋwèhel mahòhà ma mût bı̀nàm.
Nyamla wɛ̂m à nhɔ̄ɔ ŋgandàk.
Nyàndom à mɓà nyik tâ à ǹnɔl i hyàndi.
Nyàndom à yè hɛ̂dmàn i mbāy.
Nyàndom ı̄nı̄; nyàndom tàtâ.
Nyanyaŋâ à yè i njɛ̀l yɛ̂m wɔ̌m.
Nyǎŋ à ǹha nyɛ ɓàɓɔ̀blà inyùu màtèmb ma sûglù.
Nyǎŋ à nnyāambɛ man bı̀jɛk.
Nyǎŋ à nsàmbla man.
Nyàŋ à nsùglɛ man bı̀jɛk.
Nyǎŋ à yè màlêt.
Nyǎŋ jàm.
Nyǎŋ mǎn à ǹlɔ̂.
Nyǎŋ Matip à jaŋ ı̄ Kèlɓe ı̀ pam nı̀ bilɛ̂n.
Nyaŋ nyik i nnɛ̀ mɓòmôk.
Nyàŋ wâp; ɓànyàŋ ɓap.
Nyàŋgo à m̂mâl ɛ̂ŋg man i pāmnà nyɛ.
Nyàŋgo à ǹlɛndlɛnɛ mɛ ŋkono ni ŋgwɛ̀ndɛ̀.
Nyàŋgo à ǹneyēs diɓɛ̀ɛ̀ cɔdisô.
Nyàŋgo à ǹsɛɛ̄ ŋgandàk hı̀òndɛ̀.
Nyàŋgo à ŋ̀waŋ hiòndɛ̀; ı̂ni à ŋ́wāŋ kop.
Nyàŋgo à ŋ̀weŋel mɛ mı̀nsòa.
Nyàŋgo yɛ̂m ı̀ni.
Ǹyayak wee u nlɔ̀ɔ̀ u isāŋ.
Ǹyebel mût.
Ǹyèe u gweē ŋgùy.
Ǹyèe u ntùndlɛ mɛ hı̀yı̀ndi.
Ǹyèe u ŋgwɛ̂l mût gwis.
Nyèndès kɔ̀n.
Ǹyeŋ gôl à yè hana.
Nyɛ kii? nyɛ kı̀s!
Nyɛ kı̀ nû à nlɔ̀.
Nyɛ lɔ̀ɔ, ti nyɛ̄.
Nyɛ nū à ɓumbi hà!
Nyɛ nūnu à nlɛ̀hbɛ i njɛ̌l.
Nyɛ nūnu à nlɔ̀ heghèk hana!
Nyɛ̀ɛ̀ ı̀ ntı̄bil liɓùm.
Nyɛ̌mb ı̀ lep ı̀ mɓēs ɓodàà ɔk i lɔ̀m.
Nyɛ̌mb ı̀ lɔ̀na lı̀hoya.
Nyɛ̌mb ı̀ mɓāŋal ɓe mût.
Nyɛ̌mb ı̀ ǹhɔ̂gɓɛ i ɓěhnı̄.
Nyɛ̌mb ı̀ ntɔ̄dɔ̂l ɓe.
Nyɛn à mɓògna i wı̀p munu!
Nyɛn à m̂ɓôk pam hana.
Nyɛn à m̂momha mɛ ŋwɛ̀ɛ; ɓɔɓasô ɓa momha ŋwɛɛ̄.
Nyɛn à ǹhiglaha maŋgɛ ŋwɛ̀mɛl; ɓòdàa ɓa nhiglaha lep lɛ ɓa ŋɔ̄k.
Nyɛn à ǹlı̂mha mɛ̂, ki mɛ̀ ǹyɛlɛl nyɛ; dı̀ ǹlı̂mha nyɛ.
Nyɛn à ǹsêmha man i kōŋ;
Nyɛn à ǹsimha mɛ jòl jɔŋ; dı̀ ǹsimha jɔ.
Nyɛn à ǹsı̂dha mɛ ŋwı̀ı̀ u tolò; dı̀ bisı̀dha mandap mes.
Nyɛn à ǹsoha mɛ sǔglù, dı̀ bisōha i mɔ̀k.
Nyɛn à ǹtûgha mɛ bɔ̂l; dı̀ ǹtûgha bɔ̂l.
Nyɛn à ńyı̄ inyǔkı̄i à ǹcilı̄l mɛ bı̀jɛk.
Nyɛn à ńyɔ̀ mɛ mı̀ŋkɔ̀k.
Nyɛn à ŋ̀wêndlaha mɛ ŋgàŋgò; dı̀ ŋ̀wêndlaha ŋgaŋgò yes.
Nyɛ̀ŋ i Kelè.
Nyɛ̌p i ye ŋgàndàk i ŋwı̀ı̀ unu.
Nyɛ̌t ı̀ yè nùga i nnyāy.
Ǹyijàm à mpàbla ɓe hɔp.
Nyı̀i i gweē mɛ̀ masɔ̌ŋ.
Nyı̌k ı̀ m̂mâl hɛblà?
Nyı̀ŋghɛnɛ mɛ̀ lı̀kòga.
Nyı̀ŋgı̀s ɓàànɛ̀.
Nyoba u nlɔ̀na biɓuk bı̀ɓɛ.
Nyògol à ǹlɔ̂ i pōdôs mɛ̀.
Ǹyògol u njɛ̄ dinùni nı̀ bı̀nùga.
Ǹyògol u ntōba mis.
Ǹyògol u ŋkwēyha kop.
Nyògol wɛ̂m à biɓèŋha sɔsɔ̄ kɔ̄bɔ̀t.
Nyòhol mɛ̀ bı̀kààt i ɓɔ̀t.
Ǹyòl u ndap yɛ̂m u ye nı̀ ɓàkàlò.
Ǹyòl unu u gweē ɓàŋga biɓɛndɛ.
Ǹyòl wɔŋ u nsɔ̀ɔ̀ nɔp.
Ǹyòmôk u mût.
Nyondi mǎn à nnyɛ̀.
Nyondnɛ i man i mɓugı̂.
Nyòŋgol ɓěs nyɛ.
Nyǒy i mɓɛ̄p kɔɔ̀gà.
Nyǒy i mɓɔ̀ŋ wee ni mbònjı̀ i biwàdà.
Nyǒy i nhùm.
Nyǒy ı̀ni.
Nyɔ̀ maŋgèè.
Nyɔ màɔ̀k kı̀iŋgèdà mben.
Nyɔ̀ wɔŋ u ŋ́wàn ɓe màm u mpɔ̄t.
Nyɔdi hā kı̀i ù m̂ɓambāp i hyàŋgaa.
Nyɔdi hǔm!
Nyɔdi jɛ̀ɛ̀.
Nyɔdna mɛ̀ gwàà hâ!
Nyɔdna mɛ̀ hègdehègdè wɔ̀ŋ hana!
Nyɔdnà mɛ̀ mbɛ̀m yɔ̀ŋ hâ!
Nyɔ̀dna mɛ̀ wòmôl hâ!
Nyɔdɔl nyɛ̄ hâ, ɓii nyɛ̄ nyɔ̀ɔ.
Nyɔ̀nɔ i ŋkɔ̀ŋ jɛ u gweē ɓe ŋgı̂m ŋgɛŋ.
Nyɔŋ hinùni.
Ǹyɔŋ u ńyèn ɓe i pōla ɓòt ɓa ŋkɔ̀ŋ bitèk.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ a mɛ̀ màn yani nı̀ mɛ̀ mɛ̀ tibil nyɛ.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ gwèe ɓēba mbôŋ.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ mɓı̄ŋɓana ŋgı̀i bı̀kay.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ mɓı̄ŋlana ŋgı̀ı̀ bikay.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ǹlɛlɛp i njɛ̀l.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋgɔ̄ɔŋa ŋgèdà ù m̂ɓep yɔ kēk.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋkɛ̀ ɓambaa ŋ̀gwee.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋ̀kumbı̀.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋ̀kûmbnɛ i kède tùŋ.
Nyɔ̀ɔ ı̀ ŋ̀om hikɔ̀dà hisı̄.
Ǹyɔ̀ɔ̂k u têk u nnùmb lihiŋ.
Nyɔ̀piyà wɔŋ u nnùmb.
Ǹyɔyɔ̀ à ńyèn ɓe i lɔ̀ŋ yee.
Nyùgdɛnɛ mɛ̀ ɓɔ̀mbɔ.
Nyùm u gweē ŋgàndàk bilàŋ; nyùm u nsêk.
Nyùŋ à bisèes ŋgandàk hı̀òndɛ̀ mùu mbɔk.
Nyǔŋ nân; ɓànyùŋ ɓanân.
Nyùŋga ı̀ m̂ɓahlɛ mɛ jògà li nsɛŋ.
Nyùŋga ı̀ ǹtolōl mɛ̂ i ɓòm.
Nyùŋga ı̀ yè jàm li pêk.
Nyùŋga yɛ̂m ı̀ ǹtɔ̂l, bı̀ŋgɔ̀nd gwɔŋ bi ntôl.
Nyùŋgɛ̀ i ndēŋghà.
Nyùŋgɛ̀ ı̀ ŋkòyop coòm.
Nyùŋgɛ̀ lɔ̀ŋ yɛ̂m ı̀ gwèe bı̀làŋ biaâ: kwɛ̀m, kòyop, njɔ̀y nı̀ hyòdot ŋŋɛ̄mkède.
Nyùs mùdàa à ǹtı̂p gwâl.
Nyùu i ŋ̀kop mɛ dı̀sùhù inyùu ɓēba lihɛp.
Nyùu ı̀ mɓɔ̀ŋ yaga ndigi mɛ̀ jɔ̀ndɛ̀jɔ̀ndɛ̀.
Nyùu ı̀ nnyāŋ mɛ̂.
Nyùu ı̀ nsɔ̄k mɛ̂.
Nyùu ı̀ ntɔ̀mb; mini mı̀nsɔ̀ŋgi mi ntɔ̀mb.
Nyùu ı̀ ŋ̀kii nyɛ.
Nyùu ı̀ ŋ̀kwɔ mɛ̄ tùduû.
Nyùu mǎn; nyùù ɓɔn.
Nyùu mı̀nsòn.
Nyùu yɔ̀sô i m̂ɓɛt hûs.
Nyùu yɔ̀so ı̀ ŋ̀ambɛ̄ māŋ mût unu!
Nyùùha mɛ̀ ǹlamb.
Ŋ̀amb ɓàtutu à mɓèna gwelēl nsɔn we i sōŋ m̂pùyɛ̀.
Ŋ̀and u sulûk.
Ŋ̀ànɛ̀ ndap ǹlamb à ŋ̀weŋes ŋgandàk hı̀òndɛ̀.
Ŋ̀aŋ u ta ɓe jâm ndigı̂ lı̀tee ndɔ̄ŋ.
Ŋ̀aŋga u ŋkɔlà.
Ŋ̀ɛm à ŋgwēs ɓe lɔŋgɛ jâm.
Ŋ̀ɛm ŋkɔ̀ŋ, ŋ̀ɛm wɔn u ŋkàp ŋ̀kono.
Ŋ̀ɛm u hùgul Joseph inyùu mànyâŋ.
Ŋ̀ɛm u mɓēna ɓe nyɛ.
Ŋɛm u mɓoo mɛ màcèl.
Ŋ̀ɛm u nsı̄ida mɛ̂.
Ŋɛm u nsōŋgol mɛ̂.
Ŋɛm u nsōŋgoo mɛ̂.
Ŋ̀ɛm u nsōŋgoo mɛ̂.
Ŋ̀ɛ̀mb à ŋ̀ŋwehā i ndāp mɔ̀k.
Ŋ̀ɛ̀nd mı̀ŋɔ à ŋ̀kan nyɛ ǹtònɛ.
Ŋgaa ı̀ mɓām lɛ ɓalololo.
Ŋgaa ı̀ m̂ɓep.
Ŋgaa ı̀ m̂pɔt toòm.
Ŋgaa ı̀ ǹlôs ɓûm.
Ŋgaa ı̀ ǹsedēl nyɛ i ŋgı̀ holos nyuu.
Ŋgaa ı̀ yè nolol i binùga nı̀ ɓòt.
Ŋ̀gaa yes i mɓemhà.
Ŋgaa yɔn i ye jòl gwêt.
Ŋgaa yɔ̌n ı̀ ɓe nɔl ɓòt ɓa bikay i ŋgèdà gwèt.
Ŋgàbà ɓum; yɛ̀m ŋgàbà ı̀ yè tidigi.
Ŋgàdà mı̀ŋgɔndɔ.
Ŋgàdɓà ı̀ nyɔ̀ ı̀ nhōla ɓe jâm.
Ŋgàla ŋgànd.
Ŋgǎm yeē ı̀ ǹhola ɓes i pāla màl nsɔn.
Ŋgambi à yè ŋ̀kòt m̂ɓɛ̀.
Ŋgàmbi ı̀ ŋkɔ̀ɔ̀ga kı̀i nyɔ̀ɔ.
Ŋgàn ı̀ yè nùga ɓa njɛ̄; ǹten nugā lihàà li ɓaŋgòdò.
Ŋgànd ı̀ ɓèmi.
Ŋgànd ı̀ m̂ɓɛl!
Ŋgànd ı̀ m̂ɓɛmɛ̀p.
Ŋgànd ı̀ ŋkahal hɔdɔ̂l.
Ŋgànd ı̀ ŋ̀kahal hɔt.
Ŋgànd ŋwı̀i.
Ŋgànd yèe ı̀ m̂ɓɛl inyùulɛ̄ à ǹlembes ŋgandàk bı̀jɛk.
Ŋgànd yɛ̀m ı̀ m̂ɓugi inyǔlɛ̄ ɓòt mɛ̀ ɓɛ̀mbɛk ɓa ŋkɔ̀n.
Ŋgànd yɔ̌n ı̀ ǹnuhlaha mɛ̂.
Ŋgànd yɔ̀ŋ ı̀ nhɔ̄ŋ ǹlèmlèm kı̀i mbay yɔ̂ŋ.
Ŋganda lùŋ u mpedı̂.
Ŋgàndàk bı̀ɓɔ̀mb ı̀ mɓɔ̀ŋ lɛ ɓa yanàk wɛ̀.
Ŋgàndàk ɓòt ı̀ ńyı̄ liɓogɓàgà li ŋgɔ̀nd ı̀ni.
Ŋgàndàk ɓòt ı̀ nyı̄ litı̀ŋ lini lɛ ù ǹnɔl ɓâŋ.
Ŋgàndàk ɓòt ı̀ ńyı̄ litı̀ŋ lini lɛ ù ǹnɔl ɓâŋ.
Ŋgàndàk ı̀ bisèblà ndèk yɔ̌n ı̀ tebâ.
Ŋgàndàk kı̂yāga.
Ŋgàndàk nàn hɔp ı̀ ǹyobha mɛ yàk jàm mɛ̀ gwehek kâl.
Ŋgàndàk njàl kilâ!
Ŋgàndàk ǹsɔn ı̀ ntòmbhà.
Ŋgàndàk yèe bı̀tèk ı̀ ǹhedɓaha nyɛ.
Ŋgàndàk yèe hɔ̄p ı̀ ŋ̀eŋlaha nyɛ mı̀mb mee.
Ŋgàŋgò ı̀ ǹnyândlà.
Ŋgàs ı̀ yè ɓèŋel i nugā bikay.
Ŋgàtà mı̀ŋgɔndɔ.
Ŋgê à ŋ̀kembê.
Ŋgèdà bı̀ànɛ̀ bi mâl kâl i m̂mâl tagɓɛ̀, ànɛ̀ makiŋ yɔn i ye hanaānɔ.
Ŋgèdà bı̀òôm ù mpām ha ɓe ŋgi ŋgààŋgò.
Ŋgèdà kwàŋ ɓɔ̀ŋgɛ ɓa ɓe tɛhɛ ɓē mı̂m.
Ŋgèdà kwàŋ njèe ı̀ ɓeè ı̀ njɛ̄ ɓôt ɓa nhɔ̀ŋg.
Ŋgèdà kwàŋ ǹsàa à ɓê ɓe mût lı̀yanda.
Ŋgèdà lı̀lugul li moŋgō ı̀ni.
Ŋgèdà màcɛ̂l ı̀ ŋ̀kɔlà ni!
Ŋgèdà mbèŋ jaŋga li ta ɓē lɔŋgɛ ı̄ kı̀l.
Ŋgèdà mbuu u nyɔdı̂, mı̀nsòn ŋwɔ̂k mi mɓɔ̀l.
Ŋgèdà mɛ̀ yè i mı̄tı̀n hɔ̀ma, mɛ̀ nsēdi mao inyùu ɛ̄mblɛ̀.
Ŋgèdà mı̀nhyomok ŋwɛ̂m ı̀ m̂ɓaambɛ̀.
Ŋgèdà mı̀ntɛba.
Ŋgèdà mı̀ntindɛ ı̀ bitāgɓɛ̀.
Ŋgèdà mpùŋgu u nay i lɔ̀ŋ jògà li ɓôt ɓa nyuŋga li mɓēdes ndambà gwɔ̀m gwap.
Ŋgèdà mùhi ı̀ ǹtagɓɛ̀, kɛ̀ngana ı̄ nàŋ.
Ŋgèdà mùt à nı̀ŋi ɓēe, à yı̀i ɓēe isı̄, à nyondi ɓēe, wɛ̀ɛ à yè bı̀tedèe.
Ŋgèdà mùt à ŋ̀gwɛ̂l yɔm lɛ i ta hā ɓe lɛ i tɔɔhà, à nlɛ̄ɛgɛ yɔ ɓààm.
Ŋgèdà mùt nunu à ɓee mǎn, à neŋel i ndāp màjò mee nı̀ màjò mee à ɓɔy nyɛ.
Ŋgèdà ù m̂pubhànà, ù ńyı̀la mpubi.
Ŋgèdà ù ńyı̄ ɓe ɓoŋōl linı̀gà, li ŋkɛ̀gà.
Ŋgèdà yɔ̀sô ı̀ ǹtagɓɛ ɓɔ i tùk njega.
Ŋgèdi yɔ̂ŋ ı̀ ŋùnda njɛɛ ù yè!
Ŋgek ı̀ ǹtagɓɛ̀ ɓee, à lɔ̂.
Ŋgèlè yaŋɛn?
Ŋgeŋ hı̀bi ı̀ni!
Ŋgeŋ lı̀ɓàdò.
Ŋgèŋgèhi dikòa di ntòl i lɔ̀ŋ jamân.
Ŋgɛ̀gi à ŋkɛ̀ ɓigdiɓı̀gdı̀.
Ŋgɛ̀gi ı̀ mɓı̄iŋgɛ̀.
Ŋgɛ̀m yàda.
Ŋgɛ̀mbɛ ŋgɛ̀mbɛ mǎn lɔ̀ŋ ı̀ni.
Ŋgɛ̀mbɛ ū; ŋgɛ̀mbɛŋgɛ̀mbɛ ndāp.
Ŋgɛŋ ı̀ mpɔ̄t ŋgoŋŋ, ŋgoŋŋ.
Ŋgɛŋ ı̀ mpɔ̄t yɛŋgɛlɛ yɛŋgɛlɛ.
Ŋgɛŋ ı̀ ŋ̀kɔ̂lna wɛ̂.
Ŋgɛŋ lı̀ɓèdel li bijɛk ı̀ni.
Ŋgɛ̀ŋgɛyà à ŋŋwɛ̀k cɛ̂bcɛ̀p.
Ŋgɛ̀ŋgɛyà à ŋwɛ̀k juū.
Ŋgɛs pià.
Ŋgiŋgı̄bâ à gwèe ɓeba ŋ̀ɛm.
Ŋgı̀ bɛ̀lɛ̀sı̂n màtowà à ŋkɛ̀ ɓee.
Ŋgı̀ nɔk maeba nyɛn à nlēlɓaha nyɛ.
Ŋgı̀ yi à ŋ̀ûbha mɛ mbɔ̄t ŋgı̀ sɔbɛ̂.
Ŋgı̀ yi lɛɛgɛ ɓôt à ntòlha nyɛ nyùŋga.
Ŋgı̀i ı̀ ŋ̀kindɛ̄ ɓindı̀m.
Ŋgı̀i ı̀ yè hàà nı̀ hı̀si.
Ŋgı̀i ı̀ yè nɔnɔk nı̀ hı̀si.
Ŋgı̀i mbèŋ ı̀ mɓùt.
Ŋgı̀ı̀ malep.
Ŋgı̀m ɓôt i ńyı̄ ndoŋòl.
Ŋgı̀m ɓôt i ŋɛ̀mɛl hi u.
Ŋgı̀m ɓôt i ŋgi ɓanâk ɓɔ̀n ɓap koŋ inyùu wɔ̀ŋi nyɛ̂mb.
Ŋgı̀m ɓôt i ŋgi tândɓà bı̀kwèè kı̀kı̀i yı̀mbnɛ i liten jap.
Ŋgı̀m maŋgèdà m̂pɛ̀lɛ u ye bı̀jɛk bi njâl.
Ŋgı̀m mùt ı̀ m̂ɓada mɛ lı̀windi.
Ŋgı̀m mùt ı̀ ǹtɔlɔl mɛ wɔ̀m gwoo.
Ŋgı̀m ndap; ŋgı̀m mùt.
Ŋgı̀ŋgiŋà ı̀ gwèe mɛ̀.
Ŋgı̀tɔphemlɛ̀ à nhēlhàhà.
Ŋgı̀yi nyɛn à m̂ɓɔ̂ŋha nyɛ i màm mâ.
Ŋgòdò à mmɛ̀k ŋŋɔ hyàŋgaa.
Ŋgòdò à ŋ̀adap i lı̀ɓap li ndap.
Ŋgòdò à ŋ̀kwɔ ı̄sı̄ lɛ ɓùp!
Ŋgògôn à ńyèènɛ ndı̄gi i tēn ŋgògôn.
Ŋgok u biyı̀lis nyɛ jōŋ.
Ŋgok wɔn u nnyùmblahà nyɛ, ɓɔɓasô ɓa nnyûmblaha mɛ̂.
Ŋgolı̂ yèe ı̀ yè kɔ̀ɔ̀ nugā.
Ŋgolo u yeŋı̄ nyɛ̄ i tūù.
Ŋgòloŋ ı̀ gwèe ǹtàndàà jɔɔ.
Ŋgònd ı̀ ŋkɔ̀gɔɔ nyɛ.
Ŋgǒŋ ı̀ gwèe mɛ̀: nɔl ŋgòŋ.

Tòŋ i ŋkòyòp.
Tòŋ i ye kòyɓaga.
Tòŋ lilàŋ i mɓèna nɛ ŋgāndàk.
Tǒŋ nı̀ mɛ̀!
Tòŋglɛnɛ mɛ̀ màn wɛ̂m ı̀pam lɛ̄ à naŋ.
Toŋol mɛ̀ bı̀lèman gwɛ̂m.
Tòo mɛ̀ màtam ma kakaò.
Tòo mɛ̀ nyɛ mǔtàrà.
Tooɛnɛ mɛ̀ ŋgàŋgò ı̀ni.
Top, ɓoŋɛ m̂ɓèhlà.
Top màn kûŋ.
Top m̂ɓua.
Tòs nû.
Totogo i ɓâs.
Tòtòs wɛ̀m à ŋ̀obı̀.
Tɔ̀ fɛnı̂k mɛ̀ gwèe hā ɓe mɛ̂!
Tɔ̀ hɛɛ ù ŋkɛ̀, mɛ̀ kı̀ mɛ̀ ganɔ̀ŋ wɛ̂.
Tɔ̀ la kı̀i nyùs i gweē wɛ̀, nihbɛ ndı̄gı̂!
Tɔ̀ la yàa kı̀i ù ŋkɔ̀n wɔŋi, kɛ̀ nɔ̀ɔ̀dɛ kègsɛ̀.
Tɔ̀ lɛ ù yembēl nyɛ.
Tɔ̀, mɛ̀ gwèe ɓē wɛ pı̄l.
Tɔ̀ mùt à ǹlɔ ɓē.
Tɔ̀ mùt à tòo ɓâŋ i jàm lini.
Tɔ̀ njɛ ɓe nyɛn à kòli tı̄hba kwa ı̄ mbɔmbɔ̀k.
Tɔ̀ njɛɛ nyɛn à nyɔ̀ŋ ɓe hɔp i tı̀ ɓambɔmbɔ̀k.
Tɔ̀ pɛ̀s i kabā mɛ̀ hi gweē.
Tɔ̀ silı̂ŋ mɛ̀ gwèe hā ɓe mɛ̂.
Tɔ̀ ù ǹyên ŋwii ɓòo nı̀ bı̀sèp jùɛ̀m, ù galɔ̀ ndigı̂ u kɔ̂p mɛ̀!
Tɔ̀ wɛ̀; tɔ̀ laa ; tɔ̀ kii, tɔ̀ njɛɛ, tɔ̀ wɛ̀ tɔ̀.
Tɔ̀hɓana màhindi nı̀ bı̀wàdà.
Tɔ̀mb yɛ̀biyɛ̀bi.
Tɔ̀mba jâm.
Tɔ̀nà à ŋ̀òm mɛ isı̄ lı̀ɓàl.
Tɔ̀ndɛ̀ i mbondō.
Tɔ̀nɛ̀ à mɓòmla lɔŋgɛ̂.
Tɔ̀nɛ̀ à ǹtômlà; ù tòmla ɓâŋ mɛ̀.
Tɔ̀nɛ à ŋ̀om nyɛ i kòò, ŋ̀udu à ŋ̀om malêt ŋgɔ̀k.
Tɔ̀nɛ̀ à yè pèŋgel yɛ̂m i tambā.
Tɔŋ m̂ɓùmbi.
Tɔŋ nyagà i ye hēmel i masak ma ɓausa.
Tɔ̀ɔ̀ ǹtɔ̀ɔ̂k.
Tɔɔgɛnɛ mɛ̀ nyɛ lɛ a yɔ̂ŋ mɛ̀ màŋgɛ i sǔglù.
Tɔ̀p yɛ̂m ini.
Tɔs mɛ̀ kɔŋ lı̀kɔ̀ndɔ̀.
Tɔ̀tɔga jàŋ.
Tuba ǹyòl i ntōyos malep.
Tubha tùbhà njɛɛ mɛ̀ ǹtɛhɛ̂?
Tubul mɛ̀ hyèmbi; tubul mɛ̀ màpɔ̀ndɔ.
Tudu i mbâs.
Tùk ndàmb, lɛ̀ŋ ndàmb.
Tumb i hilɔga; tumb i hiŋgɔ̀ndà.
Tumblɛ̀ mût.
Tùmbul mɛ̀ nyɛ.
Tun yɔn i mɓāgal mandap mes.
Tus hı̀kùlà hi kop.
Tùtuk i nsɛ̂m, sèp i ŋkahal yɛ.
Tutup weē à ǹlem.
Tuyɛ à nhòm.
Ù bigwēenɛ hɛɛ?
Ù bilamna i sū ndi hà makòò ɓe.
Ù biyèèna nunu mùdàa!
Ù biyɔ̀ŋ hisɔ̂n ù ti ŋgwɔ.
Ù ɓa ù ŋ̀ŋwâs bihɛ̀kjùu, ɓɔ̌ŋ màm ma nnɛ̄nɛ̂.
Ù ɓàa ɓâŋ mɛ̀! lep u mɓaā jɛgı̄.
Ù ɓana ɓâŋ ɓànyambɛ ɓàpɛ.
